Min ŋaar-ak, Iisa iŋ maajirnay yeeptu pey Zeruzaleem. Iisa un̰jitu ɗo ger ka Buŋdi ho ŋa teestu atkin̰ ŋuur kuuk suugiya atta-aku. Ŋa akiliicog taabulnico ku gee kuuk maka gurus ho iŋ seesna ku gee kuuk suugiya ammaamna.
Ŋu aaɗig Iisa wiktin ta ŋa goyiy Galile, ŋu taliy kaaci. Ɗo wer-ak goy oki daaɗ dakina ku pey, kuuk coon iŋ ŋaara Zeruzaleem.
Kar ƴiriy rakki, Herood gintu iidin ta alguway. Ŋa koliig agindaw ku darrer, agindaw ku askirnar ho iŋ aginay ku Galile okin̰co.
Hiyya, daatko-at ɗuwtu geero. Min ta ote, ta gasiit romti aariɗ rasta ho ta jammiya ko ka daŋlil.
« Cokiyoŋ daŋil ta *pigiye. Ya ku tala leeginay kat eccaw ho ŋu lee, ku iban ko kadar kabuŋ gaaye.
Aariɗna loklikiiji ɗo Iisa aman : « Atikni ni ɓaay un̰je ɗo kinziirna aŋkure. »
Min ŋaar-ak di, agindaw ku *Yuudinnar ibintu kadar Iisa deliit daŋlay-at, ŋa ceera loco. Paa ko, ŋu bariy botol taat ŋuu obin̰ji. Kar gay, ŋu gin kolaw ɗo geemir. Hiyya, ŋu rasiig ŋu ɗeettu.
Min ŋu paayiy min ka dambar, Iisa karmiig maajirnay aman : « Yaman, dakoŋ kaawenno ɗo waanna ɗo maan kaak ku taltu-aŋka nam nun *Roŋ gemor, naa nooyen̰ ja min ɗo muuti. »
Iisa kaawiy pa-ak, asaan ŋu ɗiya a ŋa gin aariɗ.
Aariɗ-ak azbiig gem-ak zid-zid-zid, kar ŋa amiltu iŋ koriyay.
Iisa kaawtu pey aman : « Gem kaak un̰ja rakki min een̰ji kuuk imaanco sooɗa ɗo zunuubinnar, ŋuuji ɗuune tolo ɗo gaaƴay ho ŋuu accin̰ ɗo barrer sa guna.
Koɗok di, takan̰ mic-ak kaawtu raɗa aman : « Nu aamin kadar kii gedire ginin̰ maanna-aŋka. Kar gay, gaayorduut pey imaandu ! »
Ɗo wer-ak, gin gem rakki ŋu kolaag Yuusup min geeger ka Arimate. Ŋaar oki min agindaw ku darrer ho gee karmiyaaga. Ŋa era ase ka *Meennaw ta Buŋdi. Yuusup bal rake a zi ka Iisa yaa goye ka etor iŋ ƴiriy ta sabitdi. Ŋa ɓaawiiji ɗo Pilaat bal kolaw ho ŋa indiig zi ka Iisa.
Gee okin̰co ajbiytu, ŋu teestu kaawe benannico aman : « Way ! Taar-an garaan ta marbinto, ŋa kaawiit iŋ izinne ! Gem-aŋ awn̰a yoo ɗo aariɗnar ho ŋu karmiyaaga ! »
Ɗo ay helline wal geeger wal ɗo geray ku gee kuuk goy yeero, ŋu imiliig geen̰co ku raɗaw ɗo wer ka berel. Kar ŋu marmiliiji a ŋaa rasin̰co ŋuu diire kin bit ka kesuuney-at di. Paa ko, okin̰co kuuk diirta-at cooltu.
Ka kawtinti, Iisa saktu iŋ kawtira. Ŋa uctu min ɗo geegirdi ho ŋa ɗeettu ɗo kalaaner. Ɗo wer-ak, ŋa teestu inde Buŋ.
Hiyya, ŋu obiiga, ŋu deeyiiga ho ŋu acciig kara min ɗo jineendi. »
Iisa sin̰jitu pey uŋda sooɗ ho ŋa gasiig kun̰ Zaak iŋ siŋji Yaaya, roŋji ku Zebede. Ŋu goy siye ribbinco ka markabar iŋ tacco.
*Pariziyenna daarin̰ ɓaawiiji moota, ŋu rakiy gaase baay. Paa ko, ŋu indiig aman : « *Gaanuunte bera botol taat gem yaa totirin daaciy walla ? »
Kar Iisa indiig pey aman : « Hadi kuŋ gay ɗiya a nu waa ? » Piyer telkiiji aman : « Kiŋke Masi kaak Buŋ doɓtu. »
Ɗo wer-ak, sultan Herood adiy nigtu. Kar min ŋa togil ɗo uŋco ka geemir gay, ŋa bal nakire pey ɗo kaawoy.
Ɗo wer-ak, koɗok di, gem-ak teestu cokiye, leesey teestu awke, ho ŋa baagtu kaawe samaane.
Min ŋaar-ak, Iisa uctu min eɗe, ŋa ɓaawtu ɗo kiɗ ka Zuude, aar barre ka Zurdan. Pey gee dakin aale n̰umiiji, ŋa teestu garkiyin̰co uudin ta ŋa garkiygiigu.
Aŋ ko gamin kuuk ajbay kuuk yaa gaare a gee-aŋ aamin lotu : ŋuur kuuk aamin lotu-ak yaa gedire atke aariɗna iŋ siŋdu ho ŋuu gedire kaawe kaawin kuuk marbinto. Ŋuu obe aalna wal ya ŋu see kop taat diya sa, ginaacoɗo maanna. Ŋuu lee pisin̰co ɗo gee ku raɗaw ho gee-ak yaa coole. »
Kar ŋa ɗiyiico aman : « Ŋuur-aŋ baarir. Baar-aŋ ɗuunit *Jamaw ta marbinto taat Buŋ asiy obe iŋ gee ho kuuk min̰ ɗo saan ta gee dakina.
Min ƴiriy ta sabit birtu, kun̰ Mariyam ta Magdala, iŋ Mariyam atan̰ Zaak, iŋ gaaco Salome gidiytu itir, ŋu ɓaawiiji kockice ɗo zi ka Iisa.
Ŋu indiig aman : « Waa berjiŋ botol ki giniy gamin-aŋku ? Izinne-an, ki gasit min momo ? »
« Gem kaak garkiyaat kaaw-an, ŋa iban baati ! Ku asa tale maan ka nigindi kaak Buŋ ƴiliyo goy ɗo wer kaak kuunayɗo kan̰ji. Ya ku talga, gee kuuk goy ɗo geeger ka Zuude, illa ŋuu gaɗe ɗo baƴco ku dambiniidi.
Min ŋa taliig Iisa min serek di, ŋa iciig gaɗi ho ŋa astu dersa ɗo uŋji.
Ɗo wiktin taat Abiyataar goy *mee satkiner ka tatko, Dawuud un̰jitu ɗo ger ka Buŋdi ho ŋa teetu mappa kaak ŋu bertu *satkin ɗo Buŋdi ho ŋa beriico ɗo een̰ji oki. Zer tee ŋaar-ak, ŋuur bal gine botol taat ŋu teen̰ji, illa gay satkiner di. »
Kar Iisa ɗiyiico aman : « Jaawoŋ adiy ka kiɗar okin̰ji. Gaaron Kabarre ta Gala ɗo gee okin̰co.
Gem rakki, siŋji Yaaya, as mine gee ɗo bi ka asin̰ji ka Iisa. Ɗo bi ka Yaaya-ak ko, Buŋ kaawtu awalle ɗo maktumne ta nabi Ezaayi aman : « Nun naa n̰aame gay tabiriikar uŋci a ŋaan̰ siyin botilin̰. Gaaƴ toŋgo kaawa ɗo kalaaner aman : ‟ Siyon botol ta *Rabbiner. Siyon̰jiig botilay ɗalaŋ. ” » Wiktin ta Yaaya goyiy ɗo kalaaner, gee asiiji moota ho ŋa ɗiyco aman : « Ibinoŋ nigiŋko, rasoŋ goye kaak awalle, ŋuuko *batiziyiŋko ho Buŋ yaako saamiyin̰ zunuubinniko. » Kar ŋuur kuuk ooye, ŋa batiziyiigu.
ho seerco, ŋuu gine ar gem rakki di ɗo uŋji ka Buŋdi. Ampa-ak, ŋu seerro pey, ŋu n̰um ko gem rakki di.
Hiyya, ŋu goytu, ŋu ɗeettu werin dakina, daarin̰ miya, daarin̰ gay orok beeƴ.
Kar Iisa koliigu, ŋa deliico daŋla aman : « Maman Seetanne yaa gedire pey atke ziy ?
Hiyya, ŋu telkiiji ɗo Iisa aman : « Ni ibanno waan kaak n̰aamga. » Kar Iisa gay kaawiico aman : « Di ŋaar-ak, nun oki gaaraakonno waan kaak berdu botol taat nu giniig gamin-aŋku. »
Min ŋaar-ak, askirna iyiig Iisa ɗo geriy ka guberneer, ŋu un̰jiig atta. Kar ŋu koliig een̰co askirna okin̰co.
Raɗco ɗo daaɗ kuuk iŋ aditco ho kuuk macpi ɗo menaw ŋuur-aku !
Ŋa indiig aman : « Baaba, lociŋ-ak raɗɗo, etirit taaɓin-an minniner. Yampa, taa ginenno ar taat nun rakiyo, illa taat kiŋ rakiyo. »
Gee dakina awn̰iiji aman : « Ha’, bugam ! » Kar ŋaar gay gaaƴay jaala jaalen di aman : « Iisa *Roŋ ka Dawuud, tal aminduwir ! »
Kesuuney ta Yaaya, ŋu siyit iŋ law ku lokumi ho ŋa ɗuunit maasoy iŋ karrabin̰ ka zaami. Teen̰ji gay, ŋa eeyma bagi iŋ ƴiime.
Kar Iisa gay iban kadar ŋu bal imilin ta aditco. Ŋa ɗiyiico aman : « Maa di ku ɗibiidu ? Iyondu ja tamma rakki, naa tale. »
Koɗok di, kabarrey ta Iisa totirtu ɗo kiɗ ka Galile okin̰ji.
Kar gay nu kaawaako, Eli ŋaar as ko, kar gee gay taaɓiyig ar taat ŋu rakiyo uudin taat Kitamne kaawtu. »
Ka seener gay, gee dakin diyiiji kaaw ta raadiner, kar kaawco gay rakki ɗo.
Iisa gay telkiico aman : « Nun oki yaako indiŋko maanna iŋ kaaw rakki di. Ya ku telkidu, naako gaarin̰ waan kaak beraadu botol taat nu giniig gamin-aŋku.
« Gem-aŋ ɗiya a maa ? Ŋa nigiy biy iŋ Buŋ. Waa yaa gedire saamiye zunuubinna ? Illa Buŋ keeji di ! »
Iisa ajbiytu ɗo bi ka imaanco taat sooɗ-ata. Kar ŋa jaawig hellinnan ku moota iŋ geeger ka Nazareet, ŋa garkiyiy gee.
Darre iŋ darre asa taasin̰e ho sultan iŋ sultan oki asa taasin̰e. Werin daarin̰ kiɗ asa azire ho mey yaa ase. Ar kaak daatik aawiy atti ka weendi, gamin okin̰co-aŋ sa gaara kadar gaase ka duniiner gaaye. «
Kar ŋu jaaltu kaƴco, ŋu tala kar dambi ka tatiko-ak waan tuŋkilig ko.
Aŋ ko maan kaak *Rabbin Buŋ gintu, ho ŋa ajbiyinte tak-tak. ” »
Ta gin ta gudurriti. Min diŋ di ta kockicdu ko itir, uudin ta neginda ŋuu un̰jin̰ zir ɗo maginer.
Kar ɓaaŋ, dakon̰co kaaw ɗo maajirnay iŋ ɗo Piyer aman : ‟ Ŋaar ogirkoŋ ko ɗo kiɗ ka Galile. Anner kat, ku ɓaayiy talin̰ji uudin ta ŋa kaawiiko. ” »
Hiyya, Iisa koliig okin̰co ho ŋa kaawiico aman : « Ku iban kadar meennay ku duniiner hokumiyaag geen̰co iŋ guwaane ho aginduwco goyaaco ɗo kaƴco.
Ŋu ooyiit kaawoy. Kar ŋu teestu inde ziŋkico aman : « Ŋa raka kaawe maa, ŋa ɗiyiy a ‟ naa nooyen̰ ja aŋka ? ” »
Di ŋaar-ak, goyoŋ mento, asaan ku ibanno ƴiriy ta moo mee gerdi yaa yeepe. Kin ŋaa ase iŋ maako, ɗatik aandor, iŋ kokir ka awalle wal iŋ kawtira !
Wiktin taat Iisa n̰eptu ka markabar, ŋa rakiy ko ɗeete, gem ka cool-ak loklikiiji a ŋa ɓaa iŋ ŋaara.
Goyoŋ mento ho indiguwoŋ Buŋ kuu goye bombo ya *Seetanne gecaako. Gelbin ka gemor, ŋaar gin niyin taat ŋaa gine taat samaane, kar ziy gay gedarro. »
Hiyya, ŋu amiltu min ɗo ger ka salaaner ka *Yuudinnar ho ŋu ɓaawtu wer kan̰ Simon iŋ Andre. Zaak iŋ Yaaya sa ɓaawtu iŋ ŋuura.
Asaan min ɗo gelbiney-ak ko amiliy pikirre taat samaanno ta n̰aamiig ɗo ɓaaƴe kaak mun̰jam, ɗo kokinaw, ɗo dee ka geemir,
Ɗo wiktin taar-at, Iisa kooltu raɗa aman : « Eli, Eli, lema sabaktani ? » Ansi-ak aman : « Buŋdu, Buŋdu, maa di ki poociinu ? »
Herood gay karmiyaag Yaaya. Ya ŋa cokiy kaawoy, kaaw-at barjilaaga. Iŋ taar-at oki, ŋa el cokiye kaawnay. Asaan ŋa iban kadar Yaaya kaawa seene ho ŋa gem sellen̰ ɗo uŋji ka Buŋdi. Ɗo bi ŋaar-ak ko, Herood gooƴaag min ɗo Herodiyaad.
Ŋa taliig gee kuuk leyga-ak, kar ŋa ɗiytu aman : « Taloŋ, aŋ ko yaani ho siŋtar.
Iisa kaawiico aman : « Kuŋ gee ku diŋka-aŋ, ku geenno ho imaanko sa sooɗa. Ɗakdu mena mina naa goye iŋ kuŋko ho naako sosiŋko pey ? Iyiig roŋji-aŋ anne. »
Ŋuur gay kolaw un̰jiico, kar ŋu teestu inde ziŋkico aman : « Ŋaar-aŋ kat maa gemir kaak nam usu iŋ amay din sa karmiyaaga ? »
Pa-ak, ya Seetanne kat ello ziy ho ya geen̰ji kat kaawco ɓagɗo, gudurrey gediraaɗo taa taaye, illa taa peye.
Abaadin taat ŋu abdiyin-an, taar uca maalan di, asaan garaan taat ŋu garkiyiy gee sa, geen di imilit min ɗo kaƴco. ” »
Ɗo wer-ak, Iisa bal gine gamin dakina ku ajbay, illa ŋa lee pisin̰ji ɗo gee minaw minaw paa di ku raɗaw ho ŋu cooltu.
Kar Iisa kooltu raɗa ho ŋa mattu.
ho ansi-ak, ŋu gediraaɗo pey ŋuuco bere.
Asaan ‟ Ya ŋu tala sa, ar ŋu tallo ho ya ŋu cokiya sa, ar ŋu cokayɗo. Yampa, ta-aŋ ŋuu jipte goyin̰co ho Buŋ yaaco saamiye. ” »
Ŋu siirtu kaaw taat iy obin̰ji aman : « Ŋaar-aŋ ko sultan ka Yuudinnar. »
Ek di sultan tabirtu askirin̰ce ho ŋa beriiji izinne a ŋa ɓaa iyin̰ji kaay ka Yaaya-Batist. Askirin̰ce-ak ɓaawtu ɗo daŋaayner ho ŋa ɗukumiig kaay ka Yaaya-Batist.
Wiktin taar-at, Mariyam ta Magdala iŋ Mariyam atan̰ Zooze goy tala ɗo wer kaak ŋu diyiig Iisa.
Kun kawta, nu goy iŋ kuŋko ɗo *ger ka Buŋdi ho nu garkiyiy gee. Maa di ku obginno annere ? Kar gay, ta kuuniytu ampa-ak a kaaw taat ŋu siirtu ɗo Kitamner yaa ase ɗo werti. »
Min ŋaar-ak, koɗok di, Iisa ɗiyiico ɗo maajirnay a ŋuu n̰epe ka markabar ŋuuji ogire ar barrer aaniy geeger ka Betsayda. Ŋaar gay ɗaktu a ŋaa n̰aamin̰co ja gee-aku.
Ɗo kaaw taar-an sa, kaawco rakkiɗo.
Kar Iisa kaawtu pey aman : « Wiktin taat nu nooy gay, naako ogire ɗo kiɗ ka Galile. »
Awalle, ŋu ɗooɗgiijiig asin̰ji iŋ jinzirre ho ŋu ɗuungiijiig pisin̰ji iŋ zirŋac. Kar ŋa okiɗiig zirŋac ho ŋa kilig jinzirre. Ginno pey gem ka bombo yaa gedire ɗuunin̰ji.
Min Iisa dortu pa-ak, ŋa ɗiyiico aman : « Muusa berko botol taat kuu totirin̰ daɗitko asaan kaƴko bombo.
Ta bite-aŋ di, maajirna taltu nabiinna seer bayintu. Nabiinna-ak, ŋuur Muusa iŋ *Eli kat kaawa iŋ Iisa.
Ɗo wer-ak, romti ta Herodiyaad un̰jitu waare ɗo uŋco ka geemir. Min Herood iŋ gee kuuk ŋa koltu taliita-ak, ta ajbiygu nam Herood kaawiitit a ŋaati bere ay maan kaak ta inditu di.
Iisa gay telkiico aman : « Hii, Eli yaa ase, ŋaa leen̰ gamin-aŋ ɗo botilco. Kar ku iban di ŋu siir ɗo Kitamner a nun Roŋ gemor, naa taaɓiye dakina ho gee yaan poocindu.
Min ŋaar-ak, Iisa iŋ maajirnay ho iŋ gee dakina kuuk aaɗaaga-ak, ŋu ottu ɗo geeger ka Zeriiko. Min ŋu aaliig geeger-ak, ŋu gastu nool kaak goy oce ɗo bit ka botildi. Nool-ak, ŋu kolaag Bartime, ŋa roŋji ka Time.
Anne-ak, gem kaak luwaw, ŋaar totira kaaw ta Buŋdi. Ŋuur kuuk cokiyaat kaaw gay, ŋuur ar wer ka busam solliyo.
Nun batiziyaako iŋ amay, kar ŋaar gay yaako batiziyiŋko iŋ Ruwwin ta Buŋdi. »
Iisa telkiiji aman : « Ka seener ŋa samaane, kar wiktin yaa ase taat ŋuu ɗime, yoo dambi rakki kaak ŋu diytu ɗo giji sa goyaaɗo. »
Iisa telkiico aman : « Kuŋ kaƴko ɗibir ga ? Taloŋ, maan ka gem tiyiy-ak, ŋaar niggigɗo ɗo uŋji ka Buŋdi.
Min ŋu gasga, ŋu ɗiyiiji aman : « Gee okin̰co joriyaaciŋ. »
Isoŋ n̰ugira ho kesuun sa taat ɗo ziŋkikon di. »
Kar ŋa kaawiico pey aman : « Ɗo ay ger kaak ku paaytu, goyoŋ eɗen di nam menuwko yaa gaase. Ya menuwko gaase, kar kuu ɗeete min ɗo ger-aka.
Iisa gay ɗiyiico aman : « Ɓaaŋ, dakoŋ tala, ku gin mappa minaw. » Ŋu daktu tala, kar ŋu kaawiiji aman : « Ni gin mappa beeƴi iŋ boos seera. »
Ŋa gaariico kaawin dakina iŋ dele ka daŋlal. Ŋa kaawiico aman :
Ɗo wer-ak, Iisa kaawiico ɗo maajirnay aman : « Okiŋko, kuun rasindu, asaan ɗo Kitamner ŋu kaaw aman : ‟ Naa deen̰ gay gooƴindi ho tamgiy yaa totire. ” »
Nool-ak telkiiji aman : « Nu tala gee ar atay, kar ŋu jaawaw. »
Iisa gay telkiiji aman : « Cokay, naan̰ kaawe seene, ƴiriyta-an di, ɗo aando-anta, kokir boogaaɗo dees seer di, kii tatire dees subba a ki ibinginno. »
Kar daarin̰co gay, ŋuur ar wer kaak gin karŋiƴo. Ŋu cokiyiit kaaw ta Buŋdi ho koɗok di, ŋu ooyiit iŋ galal.
Wiktin taar-at, Iisa gay weƴa ɗo markabar aaro nam ŋa tokume. Maajirnay niiniig aman : « Gem kol tacco, kiŋ isin̰cinno ga ? Ucu ! Amay tiyaate. »
Iisa ɓaawtu iŋ maajirnay ɗo ger ka Lebi ho ŋu goytu tee. Ɗo wer-ak, gay obe miirir iŋ gee kuuk goyin̰co arro astu dakina tee iŋ ŋuura. Ŋu goyiy ɗo wer-ak, asaan min gee kuuk aaɗaag Iisa, gee ar ŋuur-aŋ goy dakina.
Ƴiriy rakki ta *sabitdi taat *Yuudinna eelgiy geero, Iisa iŋ maajirnay aaɗtu ɗo morginar. Wiktin ta ŋu biriyo, maajirnay teestu ƴiime kaƴ ku *gemer, ŋu eeymiyo.
Hiyya, ŋa baamiyiig koogina, ŋa leeyiico pise ho ŋa barkiyiigu.
Hiyya, mee satkiner ka tatko uctu ɗo uŋco ka geemir, ŋa indiig Iisa aman : « Kiŋ telkaacoɗo ga ? Gee-aŋ kaawa ɗo bi kan̰jiŋ ɗoo ? »
Ek di baarti peytu, ta aawtu ziti kadar ta coole.
Indoŋ Buŋ, gamin-aŋ yaa asenno ɗo koyin ku elgol ku raɗa.
Kar ɗubil-ak kaawiico aman : « Dakoŋ ginenno kolaw. Nu iban kadar ku bariya Iisa ka min Nazareet kaak ŋu ɗooɗtu ka etor. Ŋaar ginno anne, ŋa nooye. Taloŋ, aŋ ko wer ka ŋu diyiiga.
Gee ku geegirdi okin̰co n̰umtu wer geero.
Ŋuur gay telkiico aman : « Rabbin kat rakaaga ho ŋaako yeepin̰ji koɗok di. » Min pa-ak, gee-ak rasiigu, ŋu ɗeettu.
Daarin̰ gay sollitu ɗo wer kaak gin pompal kuuk gin jamay. Ŋu maaɗiy sawa nam pompal-ak gootiigu, yoo roŋ sa ŋu bal imile.
Maajirnay kaawtu benannico aman : « Ŋa kaawiite pa-ak asaan gi bal ice mappa-aŋ di walla ? »
Kesuuney ɗeettu portik kar nam ta diya odina. Min irn̰en di, ɗo adiy ka kiɗar okin̰ji, ginno gem kaak ya acin portik ansi.
Kar ɗo gee kuuk jalla gaminco ŋu biriy min ɗo ger ka Buŋdi sa, ŋa toɗco.
Goytu kee, Iisa jaawiy ɗo bi ka barre ka Galile. Ŋa gastu gay cabe boosir seera : Simon iŋ siŋji Andre. Wiktin taat ŋa gasiigu, ŋu caba iŋ ribbinco.
Pariziyenna iŋ agindaw ku gaanuun ka Yuudinnar indiig Iisa aman : « Maa di maajirnan̰ iciyɗo kaaw taat aginiyte rasiite ? Ya ŋu raka tee, maa di ŋu acgiyɗo pisin̰co ar kaak aginiyte ɗiyiite ? »
Ŋuur gay telkiiji aman : « Daarin̰ kaawa a ki Yaaya-Batist, daarin̰, a ki Eli, ho daarin̰ gay, a ki min nabiinna ku min awalle. »
Ta ɓaawtu, ta osiico ɗo ŋuur kuuk awalle goy iŋ ŋaara. Ŋu morkaw ho ŋu alaw.
Kar gay, Kabarre ta Gala, ŋuu gaarin ja ɗo darrinay okin̰co.
« Ku iban di, waan gediraaɗo un̰je ɗo ger ka gem kaak bombo, ŋaa soke gamnay, illa ya ŋa ɗuunig ja. Kar ya ŋa ɗuunig gay, ŋaa gedire sokin̰ gamnay bal kaawo.
Ŋaa bere maa ŋaa gidiye goye ka gaasɗo ?
Okin̰co ŋu teetu, ŋu aaytu.
Wiktin taat Iisa mattu ka etor, *Yuudinna okin̰co siya ziŋkico ɗo ƴiriy ta sabitdi. Ƴiriy taar-at teesa min gale ka pati nam gale ka pat ta kawta. Ɗo aadinco ta Yuudinnar, waan un̰jaaɗo gem ka mate ɗo maginer iŋ ƴiriy ta sabitdi.
Zaak roŋ ka Zebede iŋ siŋji Yaaya kuuk Iisa koliig oki Bowanergees, siŋ ŋuur-aŋ ɗiya aman : ‟ gee ku ar dildile ka buŋdi ”,
Kaawin kuuk ku gaariy ɗo ziŋkiko, ŋuur deet kaaw ta Buŋdi. Ku gina pey gamin dakina kuuk ar ŋuur-aŋku. »
Hiyya, maajirin ku seer-ak iyiijig roŋ ɗurkil-ak ɗo Iisa. Ŋu siddiyiig iŋ kesuunco ho Iisa n̰eptu kuwa.
Kar Iisa ɗiyiico aman : « Kuŋ bal ibine baay ta maan kaak ku indiy-aŋka. Kuu gedire kuu seen *kordindi ta taaɓiner taat naa see-anta walla ? Kuu gedire ooyin̰ *batem ka taaɓiner kaak eraanu-aŋka walla ? »
Kar gem kaak niga biy iŋ Ruwwin ta Buŋdi gay, Buŋ saamiyaajiɗo. Gem ŋaar-ak gin zunuubinna kuuk gaasɗo tak-tak. »
iŋ Zuudas Iskariyoot, ŋaar kaak asaaji isine ɗo Iisa.
Kar Iisa obtu mic rakki, ŋa iyiig ɗo ɗatikco, ŋa diyiig ɗo tumkay ho ŋa ɗiyiico aman :
Kar Piyer gay ibanno taat ŋaa kaawe, asaan kolaw obgu.
Kar Iisa karmiig a ŋu kaawenno tak-tak ɗo gemor ho ŋa ɗiyiico pey a ŋuuti bere tee.
Iisa telkiiji aman : « Maa di ki ɗiyiy a ‟ ya ki gedire kiini gaaye ? ” Ɗo ŋaar kaak aamine, botol goya a ŋaa gine ay maanna. »
Iisa taliig gem-ak ajbiyga ho ŋa elgig dakina, ŋa kaawiiji aman : « Ɗakjiŋ pey maan rakki : ɓaa gidiyig gamnan̰ okin̰co ho ɗeeɗig gurus-ak ɗo pokirnar. Paa kat, kii leen̰ mallen̰ ɗo uŋji ka Buŋdi. Kar asu, aaɗnu. »
Kar Iisa kaawiico pey aman : « Waan naallo kesuun taat zooɗe iŋ giteen kaak marbinto. Yampa, giteen-ak obaat miriŋ ta ɓokiyo ho mutti gaayiy pey tatiko.
Kar Iisa doriit kaaw-ata ho ŋa telkiiji ɗo Jayrus aman : « Dak ginenno kolaw. Aaman di. »
Yampa, ŋa ginaaɗo gem ka gerkiɗe atiydi-aka, roŋti ka Mariyam, siŋco kan̰ Yakuub, Yuusup, Zuud iŋ Simon ? Siŋtay ku daaɗ sa goy iŋ ginte annen ɗoo di ? » Taar-an ko toɗco aamine.
Wiktin ta Iisa sin̰jitu sooɗ min gee-ak, maajirnay iŋ gee kuuk goy ɗo serpey indiig a ŋaaco gaare baat ta daŋlal.
Maan ka gem tiyiy-ak, ŋaar un̰ja ɗo adiy, kar ba aaro, gem-ak ɓaay dooye. Maan ka gem tiyiy-ak, ŋaar n̰aamgigɗo ŋaa gine gamin ku samaanno. » Iisa kaawtu pa-ak a gamin okin̰co, ŋuur ku teendi.
Min ŋaar-ak, Iisa goytu keɗer, ŋa kolig maajirnay ku orok iŋ seera, ŋa ɗiyiico aman : « Ya gem kaak raka ogire ɗo uŋji ka Buŋdi, ŋaa ɗake aar ta een̰ji ho ŋaa gine gay riyco. »
Min pa-ak, Iisa coktu ka koot ka Olibiyennar ho ŋa goytu aaniy ger ka Buŋdi. Ɗo wer-ak, maajirnay kun̰ Piyer, Zaak, Yaaya iŋ Andre goy keeco. Ŋu indiig aman :
Kar ŋaako gaare ger berel ka gusuurdi, gamnay okin̰co goy ko. Eɗeŋ ko, kuute gine tee. »
Ŋa kaawiico aman : « Cokiyoŋ, diŋ gi coona Zeruzaleem. Anner ko, nun *Roŋ gemor, ŋuun berin ɗo pise ku agindaw ku gay satkiner ho iŋ agindaw ku gaanuundi, ŋuu dee kaawco a ŋuun deendu. Kar ŋuun berin ɗo gee kuuk Yuudinnaɗo.
Ɗo wer-ak, goy oki daaɗ daarin̰ kuuk aaɗig Iisa. Ŋu taliy min serek. Minninco goy Mariyam ta Magdala, iŋ Mariyam atan̰ Zaak ka kapaki iŋ Zooze, ho iŋ Salome.
Goytu kee, Iisa ɓaawtu ɗo geeger kaak ŋu koliy Kapernayuum iŋ maajirnay. Iŋ ƴiriy ta *sabitdi, ŋa un̰jitu ɗo ger ka salaaner ka Yuudinnar ho ŋa teestu ɓilde gee.
Wiktin ta Iisa garkiyiy-ak, gem kaak aariɗ obga astu. Kar ŋa teestu koole aman :
Wiktin ta Iisa amiliy min ɗo *ger ka Buŋdi, min maajirnay rakki ɗiyiiji aman : « Gem kol tacco, tal ja dambay-aŋku, tal ja pine-aŋka ! »
Iisa kaawiico ɗo gee okin̰co aman : « Dakoŋ kaawenno ɗo gemor. » Min ŋa kaawiico pa-ak, ŋuur gay totiraat kat kaaw ɗo geemir.
An ko baati ta Kabarre ta Gala, ta kaawa ɗo bi ka Iisa Masi, Roŋ ka Buŋdi.
Min pa-ak, Iisa indiig gee kuuk cokiyaaga-ak aman : « Mee jineendi-ak yaa ginin̰co maman ? Ŋa asa deen̰ gee kuuk gooƴaag jineen-aka ho ŋaa berin̰ ɗo gee ku pey.
Iisa ɗiyiico pey aman : « Ka seener nu kaawaako, min gee kuuk goy anne-aŋ, daarin̰co mataaɗo di ŋuu talin *Meennaw ta Buŋdi asa iŋ gudurre. »
Kar daarin̰ a ŋa *Eli. Daarin̰ gay a ŋa nabiin̰ce kaak ar nabiinna kuuk min awalle.
Gee dakina yaa ase iŋ siŋdu ho ŋuu kaawe aman : ‟ Ŋa nun ko Masi ! ” Ŋu asa rawte gee dakina min ɗo botilco ta samaane.
Kar Iisa piltu biy aman : « Ku astu iŋ seepinpan ho iŋ doŋkilay a kuun obindu. Wala nu kokino ?
Min paliinna yeeptu, ŋu osiiji ɗo Iisa gamin okin̰co kuuk ŋu gintu ho ɓilde kaak ŋu ɓilditu gee.
Ŋuur gay telkiiji aman : « Hii, nii gedire. » Iisa kaawiico aman : « Ka seener, kuu gedire see kordindir taat naa see ho kuu ooyin̰ batem kaak nu kaawtu.
Wiktin taat ŋu un̰jiyo, ŋu gastu ɗubil rakki goy keɗer iŋ serip ta meeda. Ɗubil-ak is kesuun portiko. Min ŋu taliiga-ak, kolaw obiigu.
Iisa un̰jitu geero, ŋa kaawiico ɗo gee-ak aman : « Maa di ku aliyo ho ku giniy hawne ? Mic-an taar bal mate, ta weƴa di. »
Iisa teestu pey garkiye gee ɗo bi ka barre ka Galile. Gee dakina n̰umiiji nam ŋa cok ka markabar, kat ŋa goytu. Geeŋ gay goy ɗo goŋgumor.
Kaawco ɗo gee-aŋ a ŋuu totire ɗo hellinniidi ho ɗo geray ku gee kuuk goy yeero, ŋu ɓaayiy gidiye tee. »
Ɗo wiktin taar-at, Iisa uctu min geeger ka Nazareet ɗo kiɗ ka Galile, ŋa dakiig gas Yaaya. Min ŋa gasga, Yaaya batiziyiig ɗo barre ka Zurdan.
[Min Iisa nooytu, ƴiriy ta dumaas iŋ kawtir kawtira, ŋa bayniitit ja ɗo Mariyam taat min geeger ka Magdala, taat ŋa atiktu aariɗna peesira min ɗo ziti.
Kar ginte gediraaɗo gii ɗiye a ‟ ŋu gee kat n̰aamga. ” Ŋu gina kolaw ɗo geemir, asaan gee okin̰co pakira kadar Yaaya-Batist, ŋaar nabiin̰ce ka seener. »
Ya gem indaako aman : ‟ Maa di ku ipirig roŋ ɗurkil-aŋka ? ” Telkon̰ji aman : ‟ *Rabbin kat rakaaga ho ŋaako yeepin̰ji koɗok di. ” »
Gee dakina leyig Iisa ɗatko, kar gem-ak ɗiyiiji aman : « Gem kol tacco, yaako iŋ siŋtan̰ goy kara, ŋu indaaciŋ. »
Min ŋaar-ak, Iisa iŋ maajirnay ottu aar barre ka Galile, ɗo kiɗ ka gee ku ŋu koliy Zeraziyenna.
Min ŋu ajimiyig ko ajimiye, ŋu cimiijit batko-ata, kar ŋu isiijit tan̰ji, ŋu ɓaay ɗooɗin̰ ka etor.
Kar Iisa gay balji telke maanna nam Pilaat din sa ajbiye.
Kar ŋa togiliitit aman : « Iŋ Buŋ, ya maan kaak ka inditu di, naake berin̰ji yoo cenne ta meennuwir oki. »
Ka seener, nun *Roŋ gemor asa mate ar taat Kitamne kaawtu ɗo bi kanto. Kar gay, raɗji ɗo gem kaak isindu ! Gem-ak, ya ŋu bal ween̰ji sa guna ! »
Iisa leesiiji ɗo aariɗ-ak aman : « Yalla bugam ho amal min ɗo gem-aŋka ! »
Kar Iisa kaawtu pey aman : « Kaaw ta gem kaawiyo iŋ maan ka ŋa giniyo, ŋuur di nigaag ɗo uŋji ka Buŋdi.
Gay riyor-at gay taliiga ho ta ɗiyiico ɗo gee kuuk goy eɗe-ak aman : « Kuŋ gem-aŋ ŋaar min ŋuura tara. »
Min ŋa dortu kadar ŋa Iisa kaak min Nazareet kat biraw-ak, ŋa teestu koole aman : « Iisa, *Roŋ ka Dawuud, tal aminduwir ! »
Koɗok di ŋu rasiig ribbinco ho ŋu aaɗiiga.
Hiyya, maajirnay ɓaawtu ɗo geegirdi. Ŋu gasiig gamin-ak uudin taat Iisa kaawiico ho ɗo wer-ak ko, ŋu gintu tee ka Paakdi.
Kaawoy-at un̰jiico kolaw ɗo maajirnay. Kar Iisa ɗiyiico pey aman : « Gem kol siŋtay, un̰je ka ɗo Meennaw ta Buŋdi, ŋaar raɗa !
Gee-ak jaawiig kiɗ ka Zenezareet okin̰ji, ŋu miniy ziŋkico ɗo wer ka Iisa ottu, kar ŋu iyiijig geen̰co kuuk raɗaw iŋ dariŋgilnico.
Kar Iisa teestu pey ɓildin̰ maajirnay aman : « Illa nun *Roŋ gemor, naa taaɓiyen̰ ja dakina. Aginay ku darrer, agindaw ku gay satkiner ho iŋ agindaw ku gaanuundi yaan poocindu. Ŋuu asiin deendu ho ƴiriy ta subbiŋkar gay, naa nooye. »
Hiyya, Iisa amiltu min ɗo wer-aka, ŋa ɗeettu ɗo darrey ho maajirnay sa aaɗiiga.
Wiktin taat yaa ŋu obiŋko ho ŋu sakkiyiŋko, dakoŋ moyenno ɗo kaaw taat kuu kaawe. Kaawin ŋuur-ak, Ruwwin ta Buŋdi yaako gaarin̰co ɗo wiktin-at di. Kaawoŋ kaaw taat ta ɗiyiiko di. Ampa-ak, ŋa kuŋɗo kat kaawaw, ta Ruwwin ta Buŋdi.
Waan kaak jammiya kara gediraaɗo un̰je atta ŋaa soke gamnay.
Min tatkaw ka askirin ku Room ka pey ɗo uŋji ka Iisa taltu maman Iisa mattu-ak, ŋa ɗiytu aman : « Way, gem-aŋ Roŋ ka Buŋdi ka seener ! »
Ŋu iyiiji. Kar Iisa indiigu aman : « Kaa iŋ siŋ kuuk siir kuwa-aŋ gay ku waa ? » Ŋu telkiiji aman : « Ku Sezaar. »
Kar ŋu teesiiji ooye aman : « Seek, sultan ka Yuudinnar ! »
Wiktin taat ŋu ɗeetiy-ak di, gee dakina ibiniig wer kaak ŋu ɓaayiyo. Gee ku min ɗo hellinniidi okin̰co amiltu iŋ asin̰co, ŋu gaɗtu, ŋu ɓaawtu ɗo wer-aka nam ŋu ogiriico ɗo kun̰ Iisa.
Gee kuuk cokiyaaga-ak ajbiytu ɗo ɓildin̰ji, asaan ɓildin̰ji-ak arro iŋ ka agindaw ku gaanuundi. Kar gay, ŋa ɓildaag iŋ izinne.
Iisa gay ɗiyiiji aman : « Maa di ki koliin a nu sellen̰ ? Ginno gem kaak sellen̰ ɗo kiɗar, illa Buŋ keeji di.
Ŋa loklikiiji aman : « Romor ta kapak raka mate. As kiiti lee pisin̰jiŋ ɗo kaati, taa coole ! »
Ya ŋa roŋ ka Dawuud, maa di Ruwwin ta Buŋdi n̰aamig sultan Dawuud meen̰ji ŋa ɗiytu aman : « Buŋ kaawji ɗo Rabbiner aman : ‟ As goy ɗo meedar nam wiktin taat naaco gedire ɗo adinen̰, ŋuu gine wer ka lee asin̰jiŋ. ”
Ka seener, gay raadindi dakina yaa ase : daarin̰ yaa kaawe a ŋuur ko Masi ho daarin̰ a ŋuur nabiinna. Ŋuu gine gamin dakina kuuk ajbay iŋ kuuk gaara gudurrico a ŋuu jage gee. Ŋuu jage yoo ŋuur kuuk Buŋ doɓtu ya ŋuu gedire.
Kar Iisa kaawiico pey ɗo maajirnay aman : « Ɗo menaw ŋuur-ak, ya taaɓin-at bire, pato yaa mate, kooy sa ceeraaɗo pey,
Ta amiliy-ak, kiɗ boosit ko. Ta teesiy ja min aaro, ta buriyiyo, ta pikiyo, ta obiy roŋ, kar kat ta niyiyo.
Pilaat telkiico aman : « Ku raka naako pikin̰ Sultan ka Yuudinnar walla ? »
Gem-ak kaawiy pa-ak, asaan Iisa ɗiyiiji aman : « Amal, rasig gem-aŋka, aariɗ ka maala-aŋka. »
Iisa niiztu puus kar ŋa ɗiytu aman : « Maa di gee ku diŋka indiy maan kaak ajbay ? Ka seener nu kaawaako, gee ku diŋka-aŋ, nu gediraaɗo naaco gine maan kaak ajbay loco. »
Ya ŋa yeep rimsilik sa, ŋa gasaakonno ku weƴe.
Hiyya, ŋuur kuuk daarin̰ ɓaawiiji moota ho ŋu obiiga.
Agindaw ku gay satkiner iŋ agindaw ku gaanuundi doriit riy ta Iisa gintu. Ŋu teestu bariye botol taat maman ŋuu deen̰ji. Kar gay, ŋu gina kolaw asaan gee okin̰co ajbiy tak-tak ɗo garaan taat ŋa garkiyiigu.
Min maajirna kuuk orok doriit kaawco-at, ŋu dapin̰iico ɗo kun̰ Zaak iŋ Yaaya.
Hiyya, Iisa iŋ maajirnay ottu Betsayda. Annere, ŋu ɗaan̰iiji nool rakki, kar ŋu marmiliiji aman : « Gem kol *Rabbiney, baan̰u ! Diirga, ŋaa pile. »
Iisa ɗiyiico ɗo maajirnay aman : « Cokiyoŋ, nu kaawaako ka seener, aaminoŋ ɗo Buŋdi iŋ gelbin rakki !
Iisa peytu, ŋa ɗiytu aman : « Koloŋga ! » Ŋu dakiiji ɗiy aman : « Obig adin̰ ! Ucu, ŋa kolaaciŋ. »
Ta taaɓiy dakina, ta jaaw ɗo gay dawner dakina, ta gaasig ka pisinti. Iŋ taar-at oki ta bal coole, baarti goy min̰a di.
Wiktin taat ŋu goytu tee, Iisa ictu mappa, ŋa deliiji barkin ɗo Buŋdi, ŋa pirsiiga ho ŋa beriicog ɗo maajirnay. Kar ŋa kaawiico aman : « Oboŋ ho taaŋ, ŋaar-aŋ zir. »
Kar Piyer gay tatirtu aman : « Nu ibingigɗo. Nu ibanno taat ka rakiy kaawe. » Min pa-ak, Piyer amiltu kara min ɗo wer-aka, ŋa peytu ɗo bit ka botildi. Hiyya, kokir boogtu.
Ka seener nu kaawaako, gee ku diŋka-aŋ mataaɗo di, gamin-aŋ okin̰co yaa ase.
Iŋ ƴiriy ta dumaas, wer dugus-dugus sabaan cokaw, ŋu amiltu, ŋu ɓaayiy ɗo maginer.
Hiyya, Yuusup gidiytu kapanne, ŋa paayiig zi ka Iisa min ka etor ho ŋa maliyiig iŋ kapanne-ata. Min ŋa maliyga, ŋa ɓaawtu un̰jiig ɗo magin taat ŋu doɗɗitu ka dambar. Min pa-ak, ŋa tuŋkiltu dambi ho ŋa ɗibiriit magin-ata.
Iisa iŋ maajirnay uctu ho ŋu ɓaawtu ɗo bi ka barre ka Galile. Gee dakin aale aaɗiiga. Ŋu asa min Galile, min Zuude,
Iŋ kawtir wer dugus-dugus, agindaw ku gay satkiner, *aginay ku Yuudinnar, agindaw ku gaanuundi iŋ gay ɗukume seriiner, okin̰co n̰umtu dee kaawco. Min ŋu deetu kaawco, ŋu ɗuuniig Iisa, ŋu iyiiga ho ŋu beriijig ɗo Pilaat, guberneer ka Room.
Kar Iisa kolsiig maajirnay ho ŋa uciiji ɗo Piyer aman : « Ɓaa annere, Seetan-aŋka ! Pikirren̰, taar arro iŋ ta Buŋdi, taar ta geemir di. »
Maajirnay ɗeettu, ŋu teestu kaawe ɗo geemir a ŋuu jipte goyin̰co.
« Nu kaawiijiŋ-aŋ, ucu, icig dariŋgiljiŋ ho ɗeet gerko. »
Iisa ɗiytu pey aman : « *Meennaw ta Buŋdi ar gem kaak liya buur.
Kar ŋuur gay bal ibinin baat ta kaawoy. Paa ko, ŋu gintu kolaw taat ŋuu indin̰ Iisa ɗo bi ŋaar-aka.
Wiktin taat ŋu ipiriiga, gee daarin̰ kuuk goy eɗe-ak indiig aman : « Ŋaar ku gina maa ? Maa di ku ipiriig roŋ ɗurkil-aŋka ? »
Gem kaak gaayaako, Buŋ yaaji berin haginey. Ka seener nu kaawaako, ŋaa gasin haginey yoo ŋa beraako amay sooɗ ku maala pondik-aŋ di ɗo saan ta ku geen̰ji ku Masi. »
Min *Pariziyenna kuuk agindaw ku gaanuundi oki taltu kadar Iisa tiya iŋ gee-ak, ŋu indiig maajirnay aman : « Maa di, ŋa tiyiy iŋ gee-aŋku ? »
Pilaat rakaaɗo nige aditco ku gee-aku. Hiyya, ŋa pikiicog Barabaas. Kar Iisa gay, ŋa ɗiyiico a ŋuu koocin̰ iŋ korɗiŋgo. Min ŋu koocga, ŋa beriicog ɗo askirnar a ŋuu ɗooɗin̰ ka etor.
Gem-ak goyin̰ji ɗo maggindi di. Yoo iŋ jinzirre oki, ŋu gedarro ɗuunin̰ji.
Kar Sadusiyenna-ak indiig Iisa aman : « Ɗo taar-an, kaawnin̰ ja, ɗo ƴiriy ta nooyindi, min kuuk peesir-aŋ, ka moo taa gine daaciy ? Asaan kuuk peesir-aŋ okin̰co midiyti ! »
Ŋu atkiy aariɗna ho ŋu etiliico sewe ɗo gee kuuk raɗaw, kar gee-ak cooliyo.
Ɗo wer-ak, agindaw ku gay satkiner isiniig gee-ak a ŋuu indin̰ Pilaat ŋaaco pikin̰ Barabaas.
Ɗo wiktin taar-at, gee asa bere siŋta ku maaniico ŋuu deen̰co ho aginay sa yaa gine paa ɗo kooginco. Koogin asa gine adin ku aginiyco ho ŋu asa bariye muutco.
Maan kaak Buŋ ɗuunga-ak, gem ipiraagɗo. »
Min ŋaar-ak, Iisa un̰jitu Zeruzaleem, ŋa ɓaawtu ɗo *ger ka Buŋdi ho ŋa taliig gamin okin̰co kuuk goy atta. Min ŋa taliigu, ŋa amiltu iŋ maajirnay ku orok iŋ seera ho ŋu birtu ɗo hellin ta Betani, asaan pat ɗeete.
Kar lokoŋ gay, ta ginaaɗo ampa. Minninko, ya gem kaak raka gine tatkaw, illa ŋaa ginen̰ ja ar gay riyko,
Gee dakina asiiji min kiɗ ka Zuude ho min ɗo geeger ka Zeruzaleem. Kar ŋu gaariig zunuubinnico ɗo uŋco ka geemir ho Yaaya batiziyiig ɗo barre ka Zurdan-aka.
Min ŋaar-ak, Iisa iŋ maajirnay ɗeettu ɗo hellinnan ku moota iŋ kiɗ ka Sezare ka Pilip. Ɗo botildi, ŋa indiig maajirnay aman : « Ɗo bi kanto, gee kaawa a nu waa ? »
Ƴiriy rakki, Iisa goy ɗo geeger ka Betani ɗo ger ka Simon kaak ɗukum burɗum. Wiktin taat ŋa goytu tee, daatik rakki un̰jitu. Ɗo pisinti ta gin ɗew ka dambir kaak ŋu kolaag albaatir. Ɗewti-ak miin iŋ itir kaak gasɗo badam, ŋu kolaag « naar ». Itir-ak, ŋu bal amsin̰ iŋ maan ka pey. Min ta un̰jitu, ta kilciit gaaƴ ta ɗewti kar ta kockiciiji itir ɗo kaay ka Iisa.
Ɗo wiktin ta Iisa amiltu ko, gem rakki ŋaamiig iŋ gaɗiy. Ŋa dersitu ɗo uŋji, kar ŋa indiig aman : « Gem kol tacco, kiŋ kaak sellen̰, naa gine maman naa gase goye ka gaasɗo ? »
Ya nu n̰aamaag aditco aaƴe, gudurrico yaa arme botildi, asaan daarin̰co as min serek. »
Iisa ɗiyiico aman : « Taloŋ gee kuuk kaawa iŋ biŋkico di ho ta aditco keetiti-aŋku ! Kaaw taat Buŋ ɗiytu ɗo bi kaŋko, taar ka seener. Ŋa kaaw awalle iŋ bi ka nabi Ezaayi aman : ‟ Gee ŋuur-aŋ beraadu horoomin iŋ biŋkico di, kar aditco gay serek min nunu.
Ɗo wer-ak, Iisa aawtu kadar gudurre amil min ɗo ziy. Ŋa kolsitu, ŋa indiig gee-ak aman : « Waa diirit kesuuner ? »
Min ŋaar-ak, ŋu iyiig Iisa ɗo ger ka mee satkiner ka tatko. Ɗo wer-ak ko, agindaw ku gay satkiner, agindaw ku gaanuundi iŋ *aginay ku Yuudinnar n̰umtu.
Kar kat, gee yaan talin nun *Roŋ gemor yaa ase ɗatik ucar iŋ gudurrer okintiti ho iŋ *darjiner.
Min ŋaar-ak, maajirnay totirtu ɗo ay wero, ŋu gaariy Kabarre ta Gala. Rabbin gaayiigu ŋu giniy gamin kuuk ajbay kuuk gaara kadar kaawco ka seener.]
Ŋu paaytu keɗer, koɗok di gee ibiniig Iisa.
Kar ŋu iyiijiga. Min aariɗ talig Iisa-ak, ŋa azbiig mic-ak zid-zid-zid. Ŋa galtu keɗer, ŋa tuŋkiliyo nam biy amila toppiyo.
Wiktin taat pat korsitu, ta aaƴiig kuuk amil-aku asaan ŋu bal paaye caari.
Herodiyaad obiijit ɗo Yaaya, ta bariya ko muutuy di. Kar ta bal gase botol.
Asaan nun *Roŋ gemor, nu bal ase a gee yaadu gine riyo. Nun as a naa gine riy ɗo geemir, naa bere zir ɗo ŋuur kuuk goy ɗo zunuubinnar a gee dakina yaa gase jile. »
Ƴiriy taat awalle ta iidin ta mappa ka bal *gele, ƴiriy taar-at, ŋu daggiy baar, ŋu gingiy tee ka *Paakdi. Maajirnay indiig Iisa aman : « Ki raka a ni ɓaate gine tee ka Paak momo ? »
Ya Buŋ kat bal peyin taaɓin koɗok, waan pakaaɗo. Kar gay, ŋa peyit koɗok ɗo saan ta gee kuuk ŋa doɓtu.
Wiktin ta maajirnay ku Yaaya doriit kabarre-at, ŋu asiig ic momtey ho ŋu tiisiiga.
Ɗak ko menaw seer di, *Yuudinna yaa gine iidinco taat ŋu koliy *Paak ho iŋ ta mappa kaak bal *gele. Agindaw ku gay satkiner iŋ agindaw ku gaanuundi bariya botol taat ŋuu obin̰ Iisa iŋ cigile a ŋuu deen̰ji.
Kar Iisa tabirtu maajirnay seera ho ŋa ɗiyiico aman : « Ɓaaŋ ɗo geegirdi, kuu ŋaame iŋ gem rakki icil jaliŋ ka amiydi, aaɗoŋga.
Muusa, ŋaar ɗiyko aman : ‟ Ber horoomine ɗo yaako iŋ takko. ” Ŋa ɗiy pey aman : ‟ Waan kaak niga biy iŋ tacco wala iŋ yaaco, tan̰ji-at, illa muutu. ”
Hiyya, ŋu riytu riyin ku iidiner, kar ŋu amiltu ŋu ɓaayiy coke koot ka Olibiyennar.
Piyer gay tatira di pey. Darum sooɗa, gee kuuk goy eɗe-ak ɗiyiiji pey ɗo Piyer aman : « Ka seener, kiŋke sa min ŋuura, asaan kiŋke min Galile. »
Wiktin taat *Herood dortu gee kaawa bi ka Iisa, siŋji alaw aale, asaan ŋu ɗiya aman : « Gem-aŋ, ŋaar Yaaya-Batist ! Ŋaar nooy min ɗo muuti. Paa ko, ŋa gintu gudurre taat ŋa giniy gamin kuuk ajbay. »
Ay iidin ta *Paakdi, guberneer Pilaat imilgiy gem rakki min daŋaayne, ŋaar kaak gee inditu.
Wiktin taat gem ka jineendi taliig ŋa as pisin̰ji aaƴe-ak, ŋa n̰aamtu ka pey. Ŋuur gay, min ŋa otiico, ŋaar sa ŋu obiiga, ŋu wariiga ho ŋu kayiig ɗo kaay.
Iisa telkiico aman : « Ku bal garkiyin̰ ga maan kaak Dawuud iŋ een̰ji gintu ƴiriy rakki taat mey diyiigu ?
Hiyya, ŋu ɓaawtu, ŋu gasiig roŋ ɗurkil-ak ɗuun ɗo botildi, moota iŋ ger ka gemor. Ŋu ontu ipirin̰ji.
Hiyya, nool-ak acciit batkoy, ŋa uctu iŋ beerin̰ji ho ŋa ɓaawiiji ɗo Iisa.
Ɗo wer-ak ŋu iyiiji gem kaak duŋguyuuyu ho gaaƴay amallo. Ŋu marmiliiji ɗo Iisa a ŋaa lee pisin̰ji ɗo gem-ak ŋaa coole.
Ɗo wer-ak, gin daatik rakki baarti taaɓiyaata. Elgin orok iŋ seer, ŋu min̰a min̰en di.
Ɗo wiktin taat Yaaya goyiy misa iŋ odinay, Herood gay obit Herodiyaad, daaciy ta siŋji Pilip. Ɗo bi ŋaar-ak ko, Yaaya kaawiiji ɗo Herood aman : « *Gaanuun baljiŋ bere botol taat kii obin Herodiyaad, daaciy ta siŋjiŋ. » Min Herood dortu pa-ak, ŋa bertu izinne ŋu obiig Yaaya, ŋu ɗuuniig iŋ jinzirre ho ŋu un̰jiig daŋaayne.
Ɗo botildi, ŋu kaawiy benannico aman : « Waa yaate tuŋkilin̰ dambi min ɗo bit ka maginer ? »
Wiktin ta Iisa kaawiyo, gee iyiiji gem ka ruŋgiye. Minninco gee pooɗ icilga.
Koɗok di, maajirnay taliy-ak Muusa iŋ Eli sawle, illa Iisa keeji di goya.
Iisa gay telkiico aman : « Kar gay, aariɗ ŋaar-aŋ, kuu gedire imilin̰ji-ak, illa iŋ inde ka Buŋdi ja. »
Min Iisa kaawa misan di, Zuudas min paliinna kuuk orok iŋ seer astu iŋ gee dakina. Min gee-ak, daarin̰ gin *seepinpan ho daarin̰ gay gin doŋkilay. Agindaw ku gay satkiner, agindaw ku gaanuundi ho iŋ *aginay ku Yuudinnar kat n̰aamgu.
Min ŋaar-ak, atan̰ Iisa iŋ siŋtay astu. Ŋu peytu kara, kar ŋu n̰aamtu gem ɓaawtu kolin̰ji.
Iisa taaƴiigu aman : « Yaman pakiroŋ ! Goyoŋ goɗom min gel ta Pariziyennar iŋ ta *Herood. »

Iisa indiig maajirnay aman : « Ku meela ɗo bi ka moo iŋ agindaw-aŋku ? »
Ŋuur gay bugum cit-cit, asaan botildi, ŋu meel benannico a ŋuu ibine waa kaak tatik paka.
Geeŋ gay goy dakina eɗe, ŋu bal gedire iyin̰ ɗo uŋji ka Iisa. Hiyya, ŋu coktu kuwa ka gerdi, aaniy ɗo wer kaak Iisa goyiyo ho ŋu noomtu bee. Min ŋu noomiig bee, ŋu paayiig gem ka ruŋgiy-ak iŋ dariŋgal.
Gem-ak telkiiji aman : « Gem kol tacco, nu karmiyiig gaanuun-ak okin̰ji min nu kapak di. »

Wiktin ta Iisa iŋ maajirnay ku subba yeepiy ɗo een̰co, ŋu gastu gee dakina n̰umco ɗo een̰co-aku. Min gee-ak, goy oki agindaw ku gaanuundi meela iŋ ŋuura.
Agindaw ku Yuudinnar n̰aamiiji gee ɗo Iisa a ŋuuji ɗibe iŋ kaawo. Min gee-ak, gin *Pariziyenna daarin̰ iŋ gee ku *Herood oki.
Min ŋaar-ak, maajirnay okin̰co gaɗtu, ŋu rasiiga.
Wiktin ta Iisa meeliy iŋ gee ku ŋu koliy *Sadusiyenna, tatkaw rakki ka gaanuun ka *Yuudinnar oki hadire. Min tatkaw-ak taltu kadar Iisa telkiico samaan-ak, ŋa ɓaawiiji moota ho ŋa indiig aman : « Gem kol tacco, min gaanuun ka Muusa okin̰ji-aŋ, ka moo paka ? »
Min ŋaar-ak, Iisa ɗiyiiji aman : « Ɗeet ko gerko, dak jagenno ɗo helliner. »
Ka seener gay, Pariziyenna iŋ Yuudinna okin̰co, ŋuur karmiya kaaw taat aginiyco rasiico. Uudin ta aadin ta aginiyco, ŋuur taaɗo ya ŋu bal ace pisin̰co samaane.
Wiktin taat Iisa kaawiy pa-ak, gee astu min ger ka Jayrus tatkaw ka ger ka salaaner-aka ho ŋu kaawiiji aman : « Romon̰ taar mat ko. Maa di ki taaɓiyiig pey *Rabbin-aŋka ? »
Min Iisa gaasiit kaawoy, ŋa uctu min ɗo wer-aka ho ŋa ɗeettu ɗo kiɗ ka Tiir. Ŋa un̰jitu ɗo ger rakki, ŋa rakaaɗo waan yaa ibine a ŋa goy eɗe. Kar gay, ŋa bal gedire cigile ziy.
Ŋa gintu menaw orok pooɗ ɗo wer-aka. Wiktin ta ŋa goyiy eɗe-ak, *Seetanne astu gecin̰ji. Ŋa goy ko iŋ kumin ku yeer di ho *ɗubal ku Buŋdi gay tala kaaci.
Kar Iisa ɗiyiico aman : « Ginno gem kaak biƴa lampa ho ŋa zuɓkiit iŋ bardila wala ŋa diyiit ba daŋlil. Kar gay, ya gem biƴ lampa-ak, ŋa diyiit ɗo wer ka jaɗaŋ.
Yampa, ɗo teesindi, Buŋ kilgiyit duniine, ŋa kilgiyig mitko iŋ daatko.
« Ni dorig gem-aŋ kaawa a ŋaa ɗimin̰ ger ka Buŋdi kaak gee pintu-aŋka, kar ɗo menaw subba di, ŋaa pine ka pey. Ger ŋaar-ak, ŋuur geenno kat yaa pinin̰ji. »

Kar Iisa ɗiyiico aman : « Ay wero, nabiin̰ce, ŋu karmiyaag di. Illa ɗo wer kaak ŋu weeyiiga ho ɗo adiy ka gerco di, ŋu karmiygigɗo. »
Kar Iisa gay taliig ƴalaaŋ ho ŋa ɗiyiico aman : « Maan kaak patiya kaƴco ku geemir, ɗo Buŋdi gay, ŋa melen̰ di. »
Ka seeriŋkar oki obiit daatko-ata. Ŋaar oki mattu bal mico. Ka subbiŋkar obiita, ŋaar oki mattu.
Agindaw ku *gaanuun ka Yuudinnar astu min Zeruzaleem ho ŋu kaawtu aman : « Ŋa gin *Seetanne kaak ŋu koliy Belzebuul ! » Ho ŋu kaawtu pey aman : « Gem-aŋ atkaag aariɗna illa iŋ gudurre ta tatkaw ka aariɗnar ! »
Kar Iisa goytu moota iŋ maan kaak gee liyiy gurus ɗo ger ka Buŋdi ho ŋa taliy maman gee liyiy gurus ɗo maanna-aka. Gay gamnar liya gurus dakina.
Kar Piyer teestu togile aman : « Iŋ Buŋ-aŋka, nu ɗiyko ɗoo a nu ibingigɗo gem kaak ku kaawiy-aŋka ! Ya nu raada sa, Buŋ, ŋaa daan kara. »

Seese Masi, sultan ka Israyeel. Paay diŋ di min ka etor, nii tale kar niin̰ aamine. » Yoo kokinay kuuk ŋu ɗooɗtu iŋ ŋaara oki waraaga.
Kuŋ gee kuuk aaɗintu gay, yaman pakiroŋ ɗo goyiŋko ! Gee asaako iyiŋko ɗo werin ku ɗukume seriiner, ŋu asaako koociŋko ɗo geray ku salaaner. Ɗo bi kanto, ŋuuko iyiŋko ɗo uŋco ka guberneernar ho ɗo sultinniidi. Paa kat, kuuco kaawin seenko.

Min Iisa taliit imaanco, ŋa ɗiyiiji ɗo ruŋgiiner-ak aman : « Gem kol roŋji, zunuubinnan̰, ŋu saamiyjiŋgu. »

kar gay, ŋu pakira ɗo goyin̰co di, ŋu bariya malle ka duniiner, ŋu diya gelbinco ɗo gamin ku duniiner. Gamin ŋuur-ak imiliit kaaw taat ŋu dortu min ɗo aditco ho ta rawtiy maala.

Hiyya, Iisa koliig maajirnay ho ŋa ɗiyiico aman : « Ka seener nu kaawaako, murgil-an ber gurus dakina pakgig gee okin̰co kuuk liya gurus ɗo maanna-aŋka,
Wiktin taat Iisa iŋ maajirnay ɓaawtu moota iŋ Zeruzaleem, ŋu ottu ɗo koot ka Olibiyennar, moota iŋ hellinnan kuuk ŋu koliy Betpaze iŋ Betani. Ɗo wer-ak, Iisa tabirtu maajirnay seera.
Min ŋu ottu, ta bite-aŋ di Zuudas sin̰jiiji moota ɗo Iisa ho ŋa ooyiiji aman : « Gem kol *Rabbiney ! » Kar ŋa baamiyiiga ho ŋa giniiji cuuɗ.
Kar ŋa kooltu raɗa aman : « Ki rakaan ginin maman, Iisa, roŋ ka Buŋ ka kuwa ? Baan̰u, nu indaaciŋ, dakin taaɓiyinduɗo ! »
Kar ŋa ictu pey *kordindi, ŋa deliiji barkin ɗo Buŋdi ho ŋa beriicota ho okin̰co seetu.
Ɗo wiktin taat roŋ-ak nee, ŋa n̰aamtu gay riyor ɗo gee kuuk gooƴaaga a ŋuuji berin haginey.
Iisa gay telkiico aman : « Yaman pakiroŋ, dakoŋ rasenno ziŋkiko ŋuuko jagiŋko.
Ɗo geray ku salaaner, ŋu el goye uŋda ho ya ŋu kolig ɗo teendi, ŋu doɓa werin kuuk taɓ.
Ŋa sin̰jitu moota, ŋa obtu pisinti, kar ŋa copiliita. Ek di ziti ooltu ho ta teestu tale kaaco.
Ŋa kaawcot ko waraŋ di. Kar Piyer imiliig serpiya ho ŋa leesiiji.
Iisa gay ooytu aman : « Hii ! Ŋa nun ko ho kuun talin nun *Roŋ gemor goy ɗo meeday ta Buŋ kaak gin gudurre okintiti ho kuun talin pey wiktin taat naa ase min ka samaaner iŋ uca. »
Ya nu ɗiy ɗo ruŋgiiner-aŋ aman : ‟ Zunuubinnan̰ ŋu saamiyjiŋgu ” wala ya nu ɗiyiiji aman : ‟ Ucu, icig dariŋgiljiŋ ho jaawu ”, taat moo melen̰ ?
« Yaman, dak kaawenno bat ɗo waanna. Kar gay, ɓaa gaar zin̰ ɗo gay satkiner ho ber *satkin uudin taat gaanuun ka Muusa kaawtu. Paa kat, ŋuu ibine kadar ki cale »
Ka seener nu kaawaako, ya waan kaak bal ooyin Meennaw ta Buŋdi ar mico, ŋa un̰jaaɗo tak-tak. »
Ŋa sin̰jitu uŋda sooɗa, ŋa dersitu ho ŋa teestu inde Buŋ a ŋa rakaw ŋaaji etirin wiktin ta taaɓiner-an minniney.
Ŋu asiiji ɗo Iisa ho ŋu taliig gem ka aariɗna obga-ak goy keɗer, ŋa coole nam ŋa is ko kesuune. Min ŋu taliiga-ak, kolaw obiigu.
Iisa ɗiyiitit aman : « Ras ja koogin yaa aaye ! Yampa, kuuniyaaɗo ŋuu icin̰ji tee ka kooginar ho ŋuu orin̰ ɗo kan̰ir. »
Yampa, ya gem kaak obit duniin okintit ɗo pisin̰ji ho ŋa rawtig goyin̰ji, ŋaar-ak galilti gay maa ?
Kar maajirnay indiig aman : « Maa di agindaw ku gaanuundi kaawiy a *Eli yaa asen̰ ja ? »
Ɗo wer-ak, agindaw ku gaanuun ka *Yuudinnar sa goya. Min ŋu doriit kaaw ta Iisa, ŋu teestu kaawe ɗo aditco aman :
Ay wer kaak aariɗji ucji, ŋa accigig keɗer nam biy amila toppiyo, ŋa eeyma saaŋji ho ziy aaƴiy yap. Nu indig maajirnan̰ a ŋuuji atkin̰ji, kar gay, ŋu bal gedire. »
Min Herood doriig kaawin-aŋ okin̰co, ŋa ɗiytu aman : « Ŋa Yaaya-Batist kaak nu ɗukumtu kaay-ak di nooye. »
Iŋ pat ta maako, Iisa iŋ maajirnay amiltu min ɗo geegirdi.
Pat gale, maajirnay iŋ markabco ot ko ɗatik barrer. Iisa gay ɗak keeji kara.
Kar gee-ak kaawiiji ɗo Iisa a ŋaa baan̰e, ŋaa ɗeete min ɗo kiɗco.
Gee-ak ajbiytu tak-tak ho ŋu ɗiytu aman : « Way, gem-aŋ gina riy samaane nam duŋguyuuyin sa, ŋa coolaagu ŋu doriyo ho gee kuuk gaaƴiƴco amallo sa, kaawiyo ! »
Gee dakina kuuk ogir diŋka yaa ɗake aaro, ho dakina kuuk aaro yaa ogire. »
Gin menaw, Iisa yeeptu ɗo geeger ka Kapernayuum ho gee dortu kadar ŋa ɗuw ko geero.
Kar ŋu iyiig Iisa ɗo wer rakki ŋu kolaag Golgota. Pa-ak ɗiya aman : « Ɗawik ta kaar. »
Min ŋu ottu wer kan̰ Jayrus, Iisa gastu gee dakina hawiyaw. Ŋu alaw ho ŋu koolaw.
Min gee-ak taliig Iisa, ŋu raastu, ŋu gaɗtu a ŋu ɓaaji ooye.
Min Pilaat doriit kaaw ta tatkaw ka askirnar-ak, ŋa beriiji botol ɗo Yuusup ŋa ɓaayiy paayin̰ zi ka Iisa.
Kogoy ta Simon gay raɗaw. Ta weƴaw, ziti kobire. Wiktin ta Iisa astu, ŋu miniiga.
Okin̰co, ŋu teetu, ŋu aaytu. Maajirna sokiig kaak ɗake nam ŋu miin girdin peesira.
Ŋa telkiico aman : « Buŋ gaarkoŋ loko maan kaak cigile kaak kaawa ɗo bi ka *Meennuwiy. Kar ɗo gee ku pey gay, ŋa kaawaaco iŋ dele ka daŋlal.
Min Pilaat dortu kadar Iisa mat ko, ŋa ajbiytu tak-tak. Kar ŋa koliig tatkaw ka askirnar-aka ho ŋa indiiga ya Iisa mat ko jammiye.
Waa n̰aamig Yaaya-Batist a ŋaa *batiziye gee ? Ŋa Buŋ walla ŋu geen di ? Telkondu ja. »
Ka seener, pokirna ŋuur goy doo iŋ kuŋko ho ya ku rakaw, nec kuuco gine taat samaane. Kar nun gay goyaaɗo iŋ kuŋko doo.
Min gem-ak doriit kaaw-at, ŋa ƴiimiit wijeeney asaan ŋa gay gamnar.
Iisa ɗiyiico aman : « Asoŋ aaɗonnu ho naako giniŋko gay cabe geemir. »
Gem kaak ɗakji-ak illa roŋji kon di, ŋa elgig dakina. Kar ŋa osiig adiy aman : ‟ Roŋdu-aŋ, ŋuu karmiyin̰ji. ” Kar ŋa n̰aamiig ba aaro.
Min ŋaar-ak di, koɗok di, Ruwwin ta Buŋdi n̰aamiig Iisa ɗo goosiner.
Gee ku ŋu koliy *Pariziyenna iŋ agindaw daarin̰ ku *gaanuun ka *Yuudinnar astu min Zeruzaleem. Ŋu n̰umiiji ɗo Iisa.
Kar ŋa rasiigu, ŋa n̰eptu markaba ho ŋa aaltu aar barrer.
Ɗo wer-ak, gee asiy asiyo nam wer arme, kara oki wer ginno. Ɗo wer-ak, Iisa gaariico kaaw ta Buŋdi.
ɗo kokine ka miday wal daaɗ kara. Ampaa ko, ŋu giniy tamaanaw, ŋu giniy motol, ŋu caaciyiy gee, ŋu giniy ta ŋu rakiyo, ŋu giniy hasuudinaw, ŋu nigiy biŋkico iŋ een̰co, ŋu iciy ziŋkico, ho ŋu poociy jipte goyin̰co.
Samaane iŋ kiɗa yaa sawle, kar kaawnar gay rawtaaɗo tak-tak.
Ta taliig Piyer oora ako, ta ibiniiga, kar ta ɗiyiiji aman : « Kiŋke oki, ki goy iŋ Iisa kaak min Nazareet-aka. »
Min ŋa mattu, zimilla kuuk ɓigira ŋu caaltu atta ɗo ger ka Buŋdi eertu min ɗatko min kuwa yoo keɗer.
Andre, Pilip, Bartelemi, Matiye, Tooma, Zaak roŋji ka Alpe, Taade, Simon kaak mala ɗo darrey,
Ya gee ku gin aariɗna talga-ak, ŋu solligiy ɗo uŋji ho ŋu kooliy aman : « Kiŋken di Roŋ ka Buŋdi. »
min Zeruzaleem ho min kiɗ ka Idume. Goy kuuk asa min aar barre ka Zurdan ho min kiɗ ka geeger ka Tiir iŋ ka Sidon. Gee-ak asiiji ɗo Iisa, ŋu dor maan kaak ŋa giniyo.
Kii elin̰ Rabbin Buŋjiŋ iŋ gelbin rakki, iŋ kelmon̰ okintiti, iŋ pikirren̰ okintiti ho iŋ gudurren̰ okintiti.
Sando, agindaw ku gay satkiner iŋ agindaw ku Yuudinnar bariya botol taat ŋuuji diye kaaw ɗo Iisa, ŋuu deen̰ji. Ya kaaw-at ɗo wertiɗo oki, ɗo tan̰co-at, ta ginaaɗo maanna.
Kar Iisa indiig aman : « Kiŋ siŋjiŋ waa ? » Ŋaar gay telkiiji aman : « Nun siŋdu ‟ Dakinaw ”, asaan nin dakina. »
Ɗo wer-ak, Iisa ɗiyiico aman : « Aaɗonnu ! » Hiyya, ŋu rasiig markabco iŋ tacco ho ŋu aaɗiiga.
Aariɗ-ak kooltu raɗa, ŋa azbiig mic-ak zid-zid-zid, kar ŋa amiltu. Ɗo wer-ak, mic-ak weƴtu lasaan̰ nam gee ku goy eɗe-ak kaawiy aman : « Ŋa mate ! »
Iisa ɗiyiico aman : « Kaawon̰co ɗo gee-aŋ a ŋuu goye ka gan̰ ka balan̰. »
Ya ŋu yeep min ɗo suuginer, ŋu aca ja asin̰co kar kat ŋu tiyiyo. Ta taar-anno di, ŋu karmiya pey gamin ku pey kuuk aginiyco gaariico ar ace ka *kordindinar, ka balsinsindi iŋ ka koŋgilgildi ku hadinner.
Kar Iisa iŋ maajirnay yeeptu pey Zeruzaleem. Wiktin ta Iisa jaawiig ger ka Buŋdi, agindaw ku gay satkiner, agindaw ku gaanuundi ho iŋ *aginay ku Yuudinnar ɓaawiiji moota.
Zuudas, kaak isinji ɗo Iisa, gaarco botol taat maman ŋuu obin̰ji. Ŋa kaawiico aman : « Ŋaar kaak naa baamiye, naaji gine cuuɗ, ŋa ŋaar ko ku rakiyo. Oboŋga, ɗeetoŋga ho gooƴoŋ samaane. »
Hiyya, Iisa ɗiyiiji ɗo et-ak aman : « Waan aawaaɗo pey roŋjiŋ tak-tak ! » Wiktin ta ŋa kaawiy pa-ak, maajirnay doraaga.
Wiktin ŋu ɓaayiyo, ŋu ŋaamtu iŋ gem rakki paa siŋji Simon. Gem-ak min geeger ka Sireen ho ŋa asa min yeero. Ŋa takan̰ Alekzandir iŋ Rupuus. Ŋu asiriig a ŋaa icin̰ etoy ka Iisa.
Min ŋaar-ak, Iisa coktu ka dambar. Ŋa koltu gee kuuk ŋa rakiyo ho ŋu asiiji.
Iisa paaytu min ka markabar. Tala kar gem rakki aariɗ obga amiliiji min ɗo maggindi.
Ŋuur gay teestu meele benannico aman : « Kar giiji telkeŋ kat a maa ? Ya gi telkiji a ŋa Buŋ kat n̰aamga, ŋaate indinte pey aman : ‟ Maa di ku poociit kaawoy ? ”
Ƴiriyo, aando, goyin̰ji ɗo maggindi ho ka dambiniidi di. Ŋa kooliyo ho meen̰ji di awriy ziŋkay iŋ dambay.
« Gem kol tacco, Muusa siirte ɗo gaanuunji aman : ‟ Ya gem ob daatko ho ŋa mat bal mico, siŋji yaa obin murgil-ata. Paa kat, taaji wee koogin ɗo siŋji kaak mate. ”
Min ŋaar-ak, gem ka jineendi-ak n̰aamtu ka pey. Ŋaar-ak sa, ŋu deeyiig kalak. Ŋa n̰aamtu gay riyor dakina ku pey, daarin̰, ŋu koocgu, daarin̰ gay, ŋu deegu.
Kar ŋuur gay, min ŋu doriit kaawti taat a ta talig Iisa nooye-ak, ŋu bal icin kaawti.
Gamin okin̰co kuuk cigile, ŋuu imilin̰co kara, ho kuuk ŋu rakaaɗo a gee yaa ibinin̰co sa, ŋuu ibinin̰co nam ŋuu talin̰co waraŋ.
Pilaat ibina tam kadar min hasuudinaw di, agindaw ku gay satkiner iyiijig Iisa.
Min Iisa taltu kadar gem-ak telkiji iŋ ibine-ak, ŋa ɗiyiiji aman : « Kiŋke-aŋ serekɗo iŋ *Meennaw ta Buŋdi. » Min ƴiriy taar-at, ŋu cimtu kaƴco cat, yoo waan sa indigigɗo pey.
Lokumo gediraaɗo taa bire min ɗo bee ka ripirrer. Kar ɗo gay gamnar gay, un̰je ɗo Meennaw ta Buŋdi yaaji gine pey raɗ paka. »
Min *Rabbin Iisa kaawiico pa-ak, Buŋ coonig ka samaaner ho ŋa diyiig ɗo meeday.
Min ŋaar-ak, Iisa ɗeettu min eɗe iŋ maajirnay ho ŋu aaɗtu min kiɗ ka Galile. Iisa rakaaɗo gee ya ibine wer ka ŋa goyiyo,
Min ŋa inde Buŋ ka subbiŋkar, ŋa yeepiico ho ŋa ɗiyiico aman : « Ku weƴaw ho ku darma misa ? Way, diŋ wiktinti nec kate. Nun Roŋ gemor, ŋuun berindu ɗo pise ku gay zunuubinnar.
Min ŋaar-ak, Piyer ɗiyiiji aman : « Cokay, ni rasig gamin okin̰co a niin̰ aaɗe. »
Min ŋu goye, ŋa sokiig mappa kaak beeƴ iŋ boos kuuk seer-aku, ŋa jaaltu kaay ka samaaner ho ŋa deltu barkin ɗo Buŋdi. Kar ŋa pirsiig mappa ho ŋa beriicog ɗo maajirnar a ŋuu ɗeeɗin̰ ɗo gee-aku. Boos ku seer-ak sa, ŋa ɗeeɗiicog okin̰co.
Ƴiriy ta *sabitdi, Iisa ɓaawtu ɗo ger ka salaaner ka *Yuudinnar ho ŋa teestu garkiye gee. Ŋuur kuuk cokiyaaga-ak, okin̰co ajbiytu tak-tak. Ŋu kaawtu benannico aman : « Kaawnay-aŋ, ŋa gasig min momo ? Ilimji ho gudurre taat ŋa giniy gamin kuuk ajbay-aŋ, ŋa gasig min momo ?
Kuŋ gay, yaman pakiroŋ ! Nun miniŋkoŋ ko. »
Ɗo bi ŋaar-ak ko, mitko yaa rasin̰ tacco iŋ yaaco, ŋa ɓaayiy n̰ume iŋ daaciy,
asaan ŋa garkiyaag maajirnay. Ŋa ɗiyiico aman : « Nun roŋ gemor, ŋu asaan berin ɗo pise ka midir, ŋuun deendu ho ƴiriy ta subbiŋkar gay, naa nooye. »
Gee-ak yaadu samtiye, ŋuudu pice uln̰a, ŋuun koocindu iŋ korɗiŋgo ho ŋuun deendu. Kar ƴiriy ta subbiŋkar gay, naa nooye. »
Ka seeriŋkar ŋa etirtu, ŋa inditu Buŋ ho ŋa ɗeeliig kaawnay ŋuur-ak di.
Hiyya, ŋu ɗooɗiig ka etor. Min ŋu ɗooɗga, ŋu ɗeeɗiit kesuuney werin dakina ho ay gem di iciy taat galji.
Miday ku tee-ak yaa nece alip pooɗ pa. Iisa ɗiyiico aman : « Ɓaaŋ kate ! »
Iisa indiigu aman : « Ku raka naako gine maa ? »
Ɗo wer-ak, ŋu isiiji batik ta dindik buŋ ar ta sultinniidi. Kar ŋu siyiiji jakumne ta jamiidi ho ŋu isiiji ar jakumne ta sultinniidi.
Ya ku gin ɗeŋgina, laaŋ ɗeŋginko samaane kuu cokiye. »
Iisa ooytu. Hiyya, aariɗna-ak amiltu min ɗo gem-aka ho ŋu un̰jitu ɗo kinziirnar. Koɗok di, min ka dambar, kinziirna-ak okin̰co eeztu tem iŋ gaɗco, ŋu sollitu ɗo barrer ho amay teeyiigu. Kinziirna-ak yaa nece ar alip seer pa.
Pilaat indiig Iisa aman : « Kiŋ ko sultan ka Yuudinnar walla ? » Iisa gay telkiiji aman : « Kiŋ meen̰jiŋ kaawit ko. »
Ta giniy pa-ak asaan ɗo adti ta kaawa aman : « Ya nu gedir diirin bit ka kesuuney-an di, naa coole. »
Hiyya, ŋu n̰eptu markaba ho ŋu ɗeettu keeco yeero.
Min ŋaar-ak, Iisa yeeptu geero. Gee dakina n̰umiiji pey nam Iisa iŋ maajirnay bal gase wiktin ta ŋuu tee.
Kar Iisa koliig gee kuuk dakina ho iŋ maajirnay, ŋa ɗiyiico aman : « Ya waan kaak rakaan aaɗindu, ŋaa pooce pey bariye galal ta meen̰ji, ŋaa icin̰ etoy ka taaɓiner ho ŋaan aaɗindu.
Kar Iisa ɗiytu aman : « Ka seener nu kaawaako, ya gem kaak rasig geriy, siŋtay, aginiyji, kooginay wala morgoy ɗo saan tanto iŋ Kabarre ta Gala, ɗo goye ka diŋka, ŋaa gase pey pak miya : geray, siŋta, aginay, koogina iŋ morgina. Wariy sa, ŋaa gase. Kar ɗo wiktin taat yaa ase neginda gay, ŋaa gase goye ka gaasɗo.
« Cokiyoŋ ! Gin gem rakki ɓaa luwo ɗo morgoy.
An gay ka aaɗaag ka awalle : Kii elin̰ giji ar zin̰ ka meen̰jiŋ. Min ku seer-aŋ ginno pey gaanuun ka pakgigu. »
Ku talig gamin okin̰co kuuk nu gintu ho ku dorig gamin okin̰co kuuk nu ɗiytu, kar kaƴko icɗo di bat.
Ŋu kaawtu benannico aman : « Gi gediraaɗo obin̰ iŋ ƴiriy ta iidiner, yampa, gee yaa barjile. »
Simon iŋ een̰ji amiltu joriyin̰ji.
Gee iyiiji koogin ɗo Iisa a ŋaaco lee pise, ŋaa barkiyin̰co. Kar maajirnay gay leesiico ɗo gee-aku.
Min ŋaar-ak, Iisa n̰aamiiga ho ŋa karmiig aman :
Kar ŋa karmiig tak a ŋuu gaarin̰jiɗo.
Uudin taat ak siyiig hadinne ho uudin taat maral giniig tiw gala, Buŋ sa icit taaɓine, ŋa newsiig gemo, ŋa giniy *cawar.
Taar ar busum ka mutaard kaak gem luwtu. Min roŋ okin̰co, ŋaar di kapak tak-tak.
Iisa kaawtu pey aman : « Ŋa Buŋɗo ka gee kuuk mate, kar gay, ŋa Buŋ ka gee kuuk goy mento. Ɗo taar-an, ku rawte tak-tak. »
Ŋa kaawiico aman : « Yaman ya ku ɓaawaw, dakoŋ icenno yoo maanna, wala tee, wala mokolle, wala gurus, illa doŋkilo.
Kar ŋa yeeptu pey ɗo maarjirnay ho ŋa gasiig ŋu weƴaw nam ŋu gedarro pilin̰ odinco, ŋu ibanno taat ŋuuji kaawe.
Yoo agindaw ku gay satkiner iŋ agindaw ku gaanuundi sa samtiyaaji ɗo Iisa, ŋu kaawiy benannico aman : « Ŋa jil gee ku pey, kar diŋ gay, ŋa gedarro jile ziy ka meen̰ji !
Iisa gay talaag di, ŋa rakiy ibine waa kaak diirga.
*Pariziyenna astu, ŋu teestu meele iŋ Iisa. Ŋu rakiiji ɗibe. Ŋu indiig a ŋaaco gaare maan kaak ajbay kaak asa min ɗo Buŋdi.
Kar Iisa gay kaawtu aman : « Dakon̰ji toɗenno. Asaan ginno waan kaak yaa gedire gine maan kaak ajbay iŋ siŋ kunto ho ba aar, ŋaa nige pey biy iŋ nunu.
Kar ŋa coktu iŋ ŋuura ka markabar, us peytu min ɗo abirin̰ji ho maarjirnay sa ta bico amallo.
Ɗo wer-ak, ŋu rakji bere maam kuuk amse iŋ dawin kaak ŋu koliy « miir ». Ŋaar gay pooce.
Ansii ko, Iisa garkiyiy gee iŋ dele ka daŋlal dakina ar taar-an di, uudin taat ŋuu gedire obe ɗo kaƴco.
Wiktin taat Iisa garkiyiy gee, ŋa kaawiico aman : « Goyoŋ goɗom min agindaw ku gaanuundi kuuk el jaawe iŋ batik ku aginda ho el a gee yaaco ooye ɗo werin kuuk gee n̰umiyo.
Iisa niintu, kar ŋa leesiiji ɗo usi ho ŋa ɗiyiico ɗo amiydi aman : « Bugumoŋ ! Yalla peyoŋ ! » Ek di us peytu ho wer siimtu dil.
Iisa ɗiyiico ɗo maajirnay a ŋuuji iyin̰ markab moota paa gee kuuk dakin-ak yaa tirƴin̰ji.
Iisa ɗiyiico pey aman : « Pakiroŋ samaane ɗo maan kaak kuu cokiye ! Buŋ yaako yeepin̰ maan kaak ku giniy ɗo geemir, kar ŋaako gaaye pey min kuwa.
Ek di rakki min maajirnay ku Iisa ceeptu seepiney, ŋa asiɗiig gay riyor kaak gina riy ɗo *mee satkiner ka tatko ho ŋa ɗukumiijit ɗeŋgey.
Hiyya, ŋu yeeptu geero ho ŋu osiico ɗo een̰co maan kaak kuuniyco botildi. Kar ŋuur gay bal icin kaawco.
Kar Iisa telkiiji aman : « Yaani kat waa ho siŋtar gay kun̰ waa ? »
Wiktin ta Iisa un̰jitu geero, maajirnay indiig aman : « Gem kol tacco, maa di ni baltu gedire atkin̰ aariɗ-aŋka ? »
Piyer gay wakiliiji aman : « Ha’a, ya nu mata iŋ kiŋke oki, nu tatiraaɗo a nu ibingicinno » Kar maajirna okin̰co kaawtu paa di.
Miday kuuk tee-ak gay yaa nece ar alip beeƴ pa.
Min ŋu ottu ɗatik barrer, maajirnay pakirtu a ŋu bal ice tee, ŋu gin mappa rakki di ɗo markabco.
Gin kokinay seera oki ŋu ɗooɗgu ɗo serpay ka atiydi, rakki ɗo meeday ho rakki gay ɗo n̰ugilay. [
Pariziyenna taliigu, kar ŋu ɗiyiiji ɗo Iisa aman : « Talu ! Maa di, maajirnan̰ giniy maan kaak gi gingigɗo iŋ eele ka geeror ? »
Ɗo wer-ak, ŋa doɓtu minninco gee orok iŋ seera, ŋa diyiico siŋ a ŋu paliinna. Ŋa doɓiigu asaan ŋa raka ŋuu goye iŋ ŋaara, ŋaa tabirin̰co, ŋu ɓaay gaare Kabarre ta Gala
Kar Iisa cooltu gee dakina kuuk gin ay biyaw ta raɗuwar ho kuuk aariɗna obgu oki. Aariɗna-ak, ŋa balco rase botol taat ŋuu kaawe, asaan ŋu ibingiga.
Ƴiriy rakki, maajirnay ku Yaaya-Batist iŋ Pariziyenna ictu sayamne uudin ta ŋu icgiyo. Gee astu indin̰ Iisa aman : « Maajirin ku Yaaya-Batist iŋ ku Pariziyennar ica sayamne. Maa di, kun̰jiŋ gay icgiyɗo ? »
Ɗo bi kanto, gee dakina asaako poociŋko. Kar gem kaak obit imaanji bombo nam ɗo muutuy gay, ŋaa gase jile. »
Hiyya, min paliinna ku Iisa kuuk orok iŋ seer-aku, rakki kaak ŋu kolaag Zuudas Iskariyoot ɓaawtu ɗo agindaw ku gay satkiner ho ŋa kaawiico iŋ maman ŋaaco gaarin̰ Iisa, ŋuu obin̰ji.
Ka seener nu kaawaako, Buŋ yaa saamiye zunuubinna okin̰co ku geemir yoo ŋuur kuuk biŋkico amila gallo iŋ ŋaara oki.
Piyer moyiit kaawoy ta Iisa ho ŋa ɗiyiiji aman : « Gem kol tacco, talig et ka ki surpiytu-aŋ aaƴ yarap. »
Agindaw ku gay satkiner diyiiji kaawin dakina.
Uudin taat ŋa cooliy gee-ak, gee ku raɗaw okin̰co akiliy ziŋkico, ŋu rakiy diirin̰ji.
Ɗo wer-ak, ŋa dortu gaaƴ kaawa min kuwa ka samaaner aman : « Kiŋke ko roŋdu, nu elgiciŋ dakina ho ki berdu galal dakina. »
Ŋaar nun *Roŋ gemor di mee sabitdi. »
Pilaat indiigu pey aman : « Kar ŋaar kaak ku koliy Sultan ka Yuudinnar-aŋ gay, naa ginin̰ maman ? »
Kar ŋa loklikiiji ɗo Iisa a ŋaa n̰aamin̰coɗo kara min ɗo darrer.
Kar daarin̰ gay sollitu ɗo kiɗ kaak samaane nam ŋu neetu. Ganduulin daarin̰ wee roŋ orok subba, daarin̰ orok bijigiƴ ho daarin̰ gay miya. »
Ku doraaga, gem-aŋ nigiy biy iŋ Buŋ-aŋka ! Ya ɗo taŋko, gem-aŋ, gii ginin̰ maman ? » Kar okin̰co ɗiytu aman : « Taar-an nec ko iye muutuy. »
Iisa obiig pisin̰ji ka nool-ak, ŋa imiliig serek min ɗo helliner. Kar ŋa giniiji ulin̰ ɗo odinay, ŋa leeyiiji pise ho ŋa indiig aman : « Ek kat ki tala maanna ? »
Min pat ottu ƴiriyo, ta mattu. Wer astu gondiko ɗo kiɗ okin̰ji nam pat subba ta maako.
Ŋu tiyaag murgilgal iŋ neendaw. Kar ɗo salaanco sa, ŋu osa kaawin dakina a paa kat, gee yaa ozilin̰co. Ɗo bi ŋaar-ak ko, taaɓin tan̰co yaa gine raɗ pak ta gee okin̰co. »
Gee dakina asiyo ho ŋu yeepiyo nam Iisa iŋ maajirnay bal gase wiktin ta ŋuu tee. Iisa ɗiyiico ɗo maajirnay aman : « Yallinte yeero, ku ɓaay ɗak jammiye sooɗa. »
Wiktin taat ŋu ɗooɗiig Iisa, pat nec parrika ta kawtira.
Naa n̰aame *ɗubildu ɗo adiy ka kiɗar okin̰ji, ŋuu n̰umin̰ gee kuuk nu doɓtu min ɗo coke ka pati yoo ɗo gale ka pati. »
Busumji daarin̰ sollitu ɗo wer kaak gin karŋiƴo ho kiɗay perew di. Koɗok di, busam-ak amiltu asaan kiɗco sooɗ di.
Kar murgil rakki pokirin̰ca astu. Ta leetu tammin seer kuuk bal baaco.
Ɗo wer ŋaar-ak, gur ku matɗo tiyiig momtina ho ak sa goy doo.
Ɗo wer-ak, maajirnay ajbiytu tak-tak, ŋu indiy ziŋkico aman : « Di ampa-aŋ gay, waa yaa gase jile ? »
Min ŋaar-ak, gee kuuk ŋu koliy *Sadusiyenna ɓaawiiji moota ɗo Iisa. Gee ŋuur-ak kaawa a gee ku mate, ŋuur nooyɗo. Ŋu astu indin̰ aman :
Wiktin taat Piyer goyiy kara ɗo wer ka berel ka gerdi, gay riyor ta mee satkiner ka tatko astu.
Min pat gale, Iisa iŋ paliinnay ku orok iŋ seer ottu.
Iisa leeyiiji pey pise ɗo odinay. Gem-ak odinay piltu. Ŋa taliy ko karaŋ.
Kar ŋu men̰n̰iig ɗo kaay iŋ eto, ŋu piciiji uln̰a ho ŋu dersiy ɗo uŋji, ansi-ak a ŋu karmiyaaga.
Gee ku diŋka, ŋuur gina taat samaanno ho ŋu newsiji kop ɗo Buŋdi. Ya gem kaak gina sokan̰ lotu iŋ ɗo kaawnar ɗo uŋco ka gee-aku, nun Roŋ gemor oki, naaji gine sokan̰ ɗo wiktin taat naa ase iŋ *darjin ta Tanni ho iŋ ta *ɗubal ku Buŋdi kuuk *cawar oki. »
Ka seener, ay gem kaak gina taat Buŋ rakiyo, ŋaar di siŋdu, boor ho yaani. »
Ansii di oki, kaak ɗeet ɗo morgoy sa yeepaaɗo geero, ŋaa icin batkoy.
Kar ŋa kaawiico aman : « Kelmol tiyaan but-but ar naa mate. Kuŋ goyoŋ anne ho goyoŋ mento. »
Iisa gay goy ka markabar di. Kar maajirnay ɗeettu iŋ ŋaara, ŋu rasiig gee ɗo goŋgumor. Markabin daarin̰ sa ɗeettu iŋ ŋuura.
Ɗo wer-ak gin ɗubil rakki kaak aaɗaag Iisa. Ŋa ginno kesuune illa ŋa kakil zimilla di. Gee-ak obaaga.
Maajirnay telkiiji aman : « Kalaan ta aŋka, kar giico gase tee momo kaak yaa necin̰co ? »
Maajirnay telkiiji aman : « Ki tala di gee tirƴaaciŋ, kar ki indiy kat a ‟ waa ga diirintu ” ? »
Ar taar-an ko, geem taat rasig mitti ho ta obtu ka pey, taar-at kokina karan di. »
Ka kawtinti, wiktin ta ŋu amiliy min Betani, Iisa mey diyaaga.
Gem-ak gay ɗeettu, ŋa daktu tees ose wer okin̰ji maan ka coolga. Ɗo bi ŋaar-ak ko, Iisa pooctu un̰je ɗo geegirdi, ŋa goytu ɗo kalaaner di. Geeŋ gay digaaji digen di.
Min siŋtay dortu pa-ak, ŋu astu a ŋuu iyin̰ gerco, asaan ŋu kaawa ɗo aditco a ŋa oliyaw.
Koɗok di, Iisa ibiniit pikirrico ho ŋa kaawiico aman : « Maa di ku giniit pikirre taar-an ɗo aditko ?
Buŋ ya barkiyin Meennaw ta asaw, Meennaw ta tatte sultan Dawuud. Ozilinteŋ Buŋte kaak goy kuwa ka samaaner ! »
Iisa ibiniit pikirrico ho ŋa indiig aman : « Maa di ku kaawiy aman : ‟ Gi bal ice mappa-aŋ di walla ? ” Yoo diŋ sa ku tallo misa walla ? Kaƴko icɗo misa ? Ŋu goy misa bombo di ?
Min ŋa indiig pa-ak, ŋa taliig gee-ak iŋ dapin̰ko, asaan ɗeŋginco amil lawa. Kar ŋa yeepiiji ɗo gem ka pisin̰ji mat-ak aman : « Taarig pisin̰jiŋ. » Ek di ŋa taariiga ho pisin̰ji cooltu ɗo weriy.
Kar gay, wiktin yaa ase taat ŋuu icin̰ ŋaar kaak obe min ɗo ɗatikco. Ƴiriy taar-at kat, ŋu asiy ice sayamne. »
Kar min gay gooƴindi-ak taliig roŋji ɓaaco-ak, ŋu kaawtu benannico aman : ‟ Taloŋ, aŋkar ko kaak ya tacco mate, jineen yaaji ɗake. Asoŋ, daanteŋga kar jineen yaate ɗake lote. ”
Kar Iisa gay buguma di, ŋa telkiɗo. Min ŋaar-ak, mee satkiner ka tatko indiig pey aman : « Kiŋ ko Masi, Roŋ ka Buŋ kaak gee abdiyiyo walla ? »
Koɗok di, min ɗo uŋco ka geemir, gem-ak uctu, ŋa iciig dariŋgilji ho ŋa ɗeettu. Okin̰co, ŋu ajbiytu tak-tak. Ŋu oziliig Buŋ ho ŋu ɗiytu aman : « Maan ŋaar-aŋ, gi bal talin̰ ƴiriy rakki ! »
Iisa ɗiytu pey aman : « *Meennaw ta Buŋdi taar ar maa ho naa gaarin iŋ daŋil ta moo ?
Min gee kuuk gooƴa kinziirna-ak taliig maan kaak kuuniy-ak, ŋu gaɗtu, ŋu iyiit kabarre-at ɗo geegirdi ho ɗo hellinniidi. Min gee doriit kabarre-at, ŋu astu talin̰ maan kaak kuuniy-aka.
Us teestu abire gidi-gidi-gidi, ŋa ŋaamiigu nam markabco sin̰jaaɗo. Iŋ ɗatik kawtira, Iisa jaawa ka amiydi, ŋa ica botilco nam ŋa gaay birin̰co.
Kar koɗok di, ŋa n̰eptu markaba iŋ maajirnay ho ŋu birtu ɗo kiɗ ka Dalmanuta.
Iisa kaawiico pey aman : « Geeŋ ke wala ŋu kilgiyig ɗo bi ka eele geeror di ? Ha’a ! Ŋu diyit ƴiriy ta sabitdi a taa gaaye gee.
Ta dortu gee kaawa ɗo bi ka Iisa, ta sin̰jitu moota min aar ta geemir, ta diiriit bit ka kesuuney.
Min ŋaar-ak, Iisa iŋ maajirnay ictu botol ta Zeruzaleem. Iisa ogiriico. Kar maajirnay iŋ gee kuuk aaɗaagu, kolaw un̰jiico ɗo maan ka yaaji ase Zeruzaleem. Iisa koliig maajirnay ku orok iŋ seera, ŋa teesiico gaare maan ka yaaji ase.
Kar ya ŋa amile ho ŋa maaɗe, ŋa ɗeetiy tatik pak gamin okin̰co kuuk amila ɗo jineendi. Ŋa imiliy leegin aginda nam ɗiiɗ sa saaƴiy geriyco ɗo leeginay. »
Ɗo mena ŋuur-ak, ya ŋu kaawaako aman : ‟ Taloŋ, Masi, ŋaar goy anne ! ”, wala aman : ‟ Ŋaar goy annere ! ”, dakoŋ cokiyin̰coɗo.
Waan laaɗo maam kuuk eelaw ɗo etirsinna kuuk taay ko. Yampa, maam-ak yaa pikin̰ etirsinna-aku, ŋuu n̰aale keɗer ho etirsinna-ak sa yaa nige. Kar gay, gee liya maam kuuk eelaw illa ɗo etirsinna kuuk marbinto. »
Kar wer kaak gee pooc obiŋko ho ŋu pooc cokiye kaawkoŋ gay, ɗeetoŋ min eɗe ho kokoŋ burintal kuuk ɗo asiŋko. Pa-ak yaaco gaare kadar ŋu gin jookumo. »
Ka seener ɗo wiktin taar-at, taaɓin yaa gine dakina ɗo geemir pak taat gee aawtu min Buŋ kilgiyiit duniine yoo diŋka. Kar ta ɗeelaaɗo pey tak-tak.
Iisa telkiiji aman : « Cokiyoŋ, koogin ku Israyeel ! *Rabbin Buŋte, ŋaar rakki di.
Hiyya, ŋu ottu kat Kapernayuum. Wiktin ta ŋu goyiy geero, Iisa indiig maajirnay aman : « Ku meela ɗo bi ka moo botildi ? »
Ŋa obiit min ɗo pisinti ho ŋa kaawiitit aman : « Talita kum ! » Ampa-ak aman : « Gem kol romoy, nu kaawaake : ucu ! »
Ŋa taltu min serek et ar buguwa lee. Iisa ɓaawtu tale ya ŋa gase roŋji. Kar gay, min ŋa otiiji moota, illa ŋa tala tapar di, asaan wiktin ta ween̰ji misa.
Min Iisa paaytu min ka markabar, ŋa gasiig gee kuuk dakin-aku. Ɗo wer-ak, ŋa taltu aminduwco, asaan ŋu ar tamgi kuuk ginno gemco ka gooƴindi. Kar ŋa teestu ɓildin̰co iŋ kaawin dakina.
Kar maajirin miintu girdin orok iŋ seer iŋ mappa ho boos kuuk ɗak-aku.
Pey daarin̰co ar wer kaak gin pompal kuuk gin jamay. Ŋu cokiyiit kaawo,
Min Iisa taliig maajirnay leesaaco ɗo geemir-ak, ŋa dapin̰tu ho ŋa ɗiyiico aman : « Rasoŋ koogin-aŋ yaadu ase. Dakon̰co toɗenno, asaan *Meennaw ta Buŋdi taar ɗo gee kuuk ar koogin-aŋku.
Pilaat indiigu pey aman : « Ŋaar nig maa di ? » Ŋuur gay koola koolen di aman : « Ɗooɗig ka etor ! Ɗooɗig ka etor ! »
Ŋa garkiyiy gee illa iŋ dele ka daŋlal di. Kar ya ŋu ɗak keeco iŋ maajirnay gay, ŋa gaariico baati okintiti.
Iisa indiig gee ku talaaga-ak aman : « *Gaanuunte kaaw a gii ginguwe taat sellen̰ wala gii ginguwe taat jookumo iŋ ƴiriy ta *sabitdi ? Gii jilguwe gee wala gii idguwin̰co ? » Ŋuur gay bugum di.
Min Iisa kaawtu iŋ daatko-at, ŋa ɗeettu min kiɗ ka Tiir, ŋa aaɗtu min kiɗ ka Sidon iŋ kiɗ kaak ŋu koliy Geegirnay ku Orok ho ŋa birtu ɗo biy barre ka Galile.
Wiktin ta Iisa rasiig gee ŋa un̰jitu geero, maajirnay indiig aman : « Gaarnin̰ ja baat ta daŋlal-anta. »
Paa ko, Dawuud meen̰ji oki kolaag Masi-ak a ‟ Rabbine ”. Di maman ŋaa gine roŋji ? » Wiktin ta ŋa kaawiy pa-ak, gee dakina goya. Kaawoy-at ginco gala.
Taloŋ, gem kaak isindu-aŋ asa ko eka ! Ucoŋ, ŋaaminteŋga ! »
Gee dakina ɓaawiiji ɗo Pilaat. Ŋu teestu indin̰ji a ŋaaco gine maan kaak ŋa gingiyco ay iidin ta Paakdi.
Hiyya, Iisa ɗeettu iŋ ŋaara. Gee dakina aaɗiigu nam ŋu tirƴaaga.
Wiktin ta Iisa garkiyiy gee ɗo *ger ka Buŋdi, ŋa ɗiy aman : « Maman agindaw ku gaanuundi kaawiy a Masi ŋaar roŋ ka Dawuud ?
Min Piyer kaawa misan di, uc gootiigu ho min ɗo uc-at amila gaaƴ kaawa aman : « Ŋaar-aŋ Roŋdu, nu elgig dakina. Cokiyon kaawoy ! »
Hiyya, okin̰co siŋta ku peesir-ak obiita ho ŋu siibiytu bal koogina. Ba aaro, taar sa menuwti gaastu. »
Kar ŋa koliig Piyer, Zaak iŋ Yaaya. Ɗo wer-ak, kelmoy amiltu ho ziy sa oolga.
Yaman pakiroŋ, goyoŋ mento asaan ku ibanno kimin wiktin-at yaa ase.
Hiyya, Iisa obiig min ɗo pisin̰ji, ŋa copiliiga ho mic-ak peytu.
Ɗo ger kaak ŋaa un̰je, kaawon̰ji ɗo mee ka gerdi-ak aman : ‟ Tatkaw n̰aaminti a niin̰ inde wer kaak ŋaa tee tee ka iidiner iŋ maajirnay ? ”
Gem rakki min ɗatik geemir ɗiyiiji aman : « Gem kol tacco, nu iyjiŋ roŋdu, kiidu coolin̰ji. Ŋa gin aariɗ ka toɗaaji kaawo.
Hiyya, ba aar Iisa bayniico ɗo maajirnay kuuk orok iŋ rakki ɗo wiktin ta ŋu tiyiyo. Ŋa leesiico ɗo bi ka imaanco taat sooɗa ho iŋ kaƴco kuuk bombo, ŋu icgiyɗo kaaw ta gee kuuk talig ŋa nooye.
Gem kaak gin burɗum asiiji ɗo Iisa. Ŋa dersitu ɗo uŋji, ŋa loklikiiji aman : « Gem kol Rabbiney, kiin gedire calindu ya ki ooye. »
Min ŋaar-ak, ŋa yeepiico ɗo maajirnay kuuk subba. Kar ŋa gasiig ŋu weƴaw. Ŋa kaawiiji ɗo Piyer aman : « Simon, ki weƴa ga ! Ki bal gedire goye mento pat rakki di oki ?
« Wayyay, Iisa ka min Nazareet, ki rakaani gine maman ? Ki asinti ide walla ? Nun iban tam kadar kiŋke gem kaak Buŋ doɓtu ho ŋa n̰aamtu. »
Ŋa ɗiyiico aman : « Ɓaaŋ ɗo hellin ta goy uŋda-antare. Ya ku ote, kuu gase roŋ ɗurkilal ɗuune. Ƴiriy rakki waan bal n̰epin̰ji. Ipiroŋga ho iyoŋduuga.
Daatko-at kaawiiji aman : « Gem kol *Rabbiney, kaawon̰-an ka seener. Kar kan̰ sa, ŋuur tiya meerin kuuk gaama min ɗo pise ku kooginar di. »
Iisa indiig aman : « Ku gin mappa minaw ? » Ŋuur gay aman : « Ni gin mappa peesira »
Min ŋaar-ak, Iisa teesiico dele daŋla ɗo agindaw ku *Yuudinnar aman : « Gin mee jineendi rakki. Ŋa taattu atay kuuk ŋu koliy *bin̰ ɗo jineen-aka ho ŋa ŋaamiig iŋ kelel. Ŋa siytu dukitka taat ŋuu miƴin̰ roŋ ku atiydi-aku. Kar ŋa pintu ger bolok a ŋuu coke kuwa ŋuu gooƴin̰ji. Hiyya, ŋa rasig jineen-ak ɗo gee daarin̰ a ŋuu gooƴin̰ji ho ŋa ɗeettu marti.
Ŋuur-aŋ ko gamin ku samaanno kuuk amila min ɗo adiy ka gemor, ho nigaag ɗo uŋji ka Buŋdi. »
Tala kar daatik rakki romti aariɗ obta dortu gee kaawa ɗo bi ka Iisa, ta asiiji. Taar gay Yuudin̰caɗo, ŋu weeyit ɗo geeger Siri ɗo ka kiɗ ka Penisi. Min ta asiiji, ta dersitu ɗo uŋji ho ta marmiliiji aman : « Gem kol tacco, baan̰u ! Atkig aariɗ-aŋ min ɗo romor. »
Wiktin ta Iisa imiliy kaay min ɗo amiydi, ŋa taliig samaan pil waakilak. Kar Ruwwin ta Buŋdi paayiiji ar ammaama.
Kar Iisa ɗiyiico aman : « Ku ibanno baat ta daŋlal-anta walla ? Kar di maman kuu ibine baat ta daŋlal ta pey ?
Hiyya, Piyer kaawiiji ɗo Iisa aman : « Gem kol tacco, gala ni goyiy anne-aŋka. Niiko siye tarram subba, rakki locin, rakki ɗo Muusa ho rakki gay ɗo Eli. »
Min ŋaar-ak, Iisa obiig gem-aka, ŋa imiliig serek min ɗo geemir ho ŋa koln̰iijig ɗeŋginay ku gem-ak iŋ kormay, kar ŋa pictu uln̰a ɗo kormay ho ŋa diirijiit leesey ta gem-aka.
Aŋ ko siŋco ku paliinnar kuuk orok iŋ seera : Simon kaak Iisa koliig oki Piyer,
Ɗum woni puɗɗooɗe Kabaaru Lobbo haala Iisaa AlmasiihuƁii Laamɗo oo.
Nii winndorii e dewtere annabi Esaaya: «Miin Laamɗo, mi ardinante nelaaɗo am moƴƴinanoowo ma laawol.
Neɗɗo ana ooynoo ley ladde jeereende: Moƴƴinee laawol Joomiraaɗo ngol, ndartinee ɗati makko.»
Oon nelaaɗo woni Yaayaa lootoowo lootogal batisima oo. O ɓanngi ley ladde jeereende, omo ooynoo omo wiya yimɓe tuuba, mbatisee yalla luutti mum'en ana njaafee.
Yimɓe leydi Yahuudiya e yimɓe Urusaliima fuu ngari, njaadiri luutti mum'en, Yaayaa looti ɓe lootogal batisima ley maayo Urdun.
Yaayaa, kaddule ɗe leeɓi gelooɗi ɓoornotonoo, humoo nguruwol, buureeti e njumri ladde o wuuri.
Omo waajoroo daande toownde, omo wiya: —Ɓurɗo kam baawɗe waran caggal am, mi fotaa fay turaade mi humta ɓoggi paɗe makko.
Miin, ndiyam mbatisir-mi on, kaa kanko, Ruuhu Ceniiɗo o batisirta on.
Ley ɗeen ɲalaaɗe, Iisaa iwi ngeenndi Nasaraatu ley leydi Galili, wari, Yaayaabatisi mo ley maayo Urdun.
Wakkati o ƴeentata ndiyam ɗam oo, o yii kammu udditike, o yii Ruuhu Ceniiɗo ana jippoo e makko hono no wuugaandu nii.
Daande iwnde dow kammu ooynii, wii: —Aan woni Ɓiyam mo korsin-mi, aan cuɓii-mi.
Oon wakkati fuu, Ruuhu naɓi mo ley ladde jeereende.
O waɗi ton balɗe capanɗe nay, Ibiliisa ana tewta seytaade mo, omo hakkunde kulle ladde, malaa'ika'en ana ngollana mo.
Caggal uddeede Yaayaa ley kasu, Iisaa yehi Galili ana waajoo Kabaaru Lobbo haala Laamɗo,
ana wiya: —Wakkati oo warii, Laamu Laamɗo ɓattiima. Tuubee, ngoonɗinee Kabaaru Lobbo.
Iisaa ana yahannoo dow fonngo weendu Galili, non yii Simon e miɲum Andire ana tippoo bubbi mum'en ley weendu nduu yo awooɓe.
Iisaa wii ɓe: —Njokkee kam, mi waɗa on awooɓe yimɓe.
Ɗon e ɗon ɓe njoppi bubbi maɓɓe ɗii, ɓe njokki e makko.
O yehi yeeso seeɗa, o yii Yaakuuba ɓii Jebede e miɲum Yuhanna ley laana mum'en ana moƴƴintina bubbi.
Oon wakkati fuu, o noddi ɓe. Ɓe njoppi baam maɓɓe Jebede, kaɲum e hasaaɓe ɓee ley laana kaa, ɓe njokki e makko.
Caggal ɗum, ɓe njehi ngeenndi mbiyeteendi Kafarnahum, Iisaa naati suudu waajordu, fuɗɗi waajaade. Ɲannde mum yo fowteteende.
Tawaaɓe ɗon ɓee kaaynaa e waaju makko oo, sabi o waajorike ɓe no jom baawɗe nii, wanaa no dunkee'en Sariya nii.
Gorko laddaaɗo ana e waajordu nduu, wulli,
wii: —Iisaa Nasaraatunke oo, koɗum hillu maa e amen? A garɗo halkude min naa? Miɗo anndi ko ngon-ɗaa, a ceniiɗo iwruɗo to Laamɗo!
Iisaa jahii e seyɗaani oo, wii: —Deƴƴu yaltu e makko!
Seyɗaani oo dimmbi gorko oo semmbe, wulli wullaango toowngo, yalti e makko.
Jamaa oo fuu haaynaa, hedde ana lamndondira: —Ko ɗum woni? Ɗum anndal kesal koy! Omo yamira fay seyɗaani'en ɓee, ɓe ɗowtanto mo.
Wakkati gooto kabaaru makko saakii ley leydi Galili fuu.
Nde ɓe njaltunoo waajordu nduu ndee, ɓe njehi galle Simon e Andire. Yaakuuba e Yuhanna njaadi e maɓɓe.
Esii Simon debbo ana lelii yo jontaaɗo. Iisaa yottii tan, haalanaa haala makko,
ɓattitii mo, nanngi junngo makko, immini mo. Ɗon e ɗon jontere makko selli, o laatanii ɓe njaatigi.
Kiikiiɗe caggal janal naange, yimɓe ngaddani Iisaa ɲawɓe e laddaaɓe fuu.
Ngeenndi ndii fuu hawriti dow damal ngal.
O sellini ɲawɓe heewɓe, ɲawɓe ɲawuuji ɗi ngaldaa sii. O ribbi seyɗaani'en heewɓe, o accataa seyɗaani'en ɓee kaala, sabi eɓe anndi ko mo woni jaati.
Janngo mum, Iisaa hujji gila law, yehi nokku teelɗo ana waɗa ton duwaawu.
Simon e wondiiɓe mum ndarii ana tewta mo.
Nde ɓe njiiti mo ndee, ɓe mbii mo: —Yimɓe fuu ana ndaarte.
Iisaa wii ɓe: —Njehen ley geelle ɓadiiɗe ɗee faa mi waajoo ton duu, sabi ɗum waddi kam.
O yehi ley leydi Galili fuu, omo waajoo ley cuuɗi baajorɗi maɓɓe, omo ribba seyɗaani'en.
Gorko ceppaaɗo wari diccii yeeso makko, ndaardi mo, wii: —So tawii a jaɓii, aɗa waawi sellinde kam!
Iisaa yurminaa, foocci junngo mum, memi mo, wii: —Mi jaɓii, sellu!
Ɗon e ɗon, ceppe ɗee iwi e gorko oo, o selli.
Oon wakkati fuu, Iisaa yoppiti mo, daalii mo,
wii: —Haya koy, pati humpitin fay gooto, yaa holloy hoore maa jottinoowo sadaka, ngaɗanaa laaɓugol maa ngol sadaka mo Muusaa yamiri oo faa anndina ɓe a sellii.
Kaa kanko, o iwi ɗon tan, o darii omo saaka kabaaru oo. Ɗum waɗi so Iisaa ronki naatude geelle, heddii ladde, yimɓe ana iwra tatteeji fuu ana ngara e mum.
Caggal balɗe seeɗa, Iisaa warti ngeenndi Kafarnahum. Yimɓe nani omo cuuɗi.
Jamaa keewɗo hawriti ɗon faa fay nokkuure heddaaki, wanaa haala yeeso damal ngal, hedde omo waajoo ɓe konngol Laamɗo ngol.
Yimɓe ngari, ngaddani mo bonnguujo mo worɓe nayon ndoondii.
Kaa ɓe ndonkii yottinde mo Iisaa sabaabu jamaa oo. Ɗum waɗi so ɓe kippiti bene oo foonndo makko, ɓe njippiniri bonnguujo oo e yulannde ndee, tawi ana lelnaa e dengeleewo.
Nde Iisaa yiinoo goonɗinal maɓɓe ndee, wii bonnguujo oo: —Giɗam, luutti maa njaafaama.
Dunkee'en Sariya jooɗinooɓe ɗon ɓee ndarii ana miiloo e ɓerɗe mum'en:
«Hono oo gorko haaldi ɗum? O bonkike Laamɗo! Homo waawi yaafaade luutti so wanaa Laamɗo gooto oo?»
Iisaa faami ɗon e ɗon miilooji maɓɓe, wii ɓe: —Koɗum waɗi so oɗon miiloo miilooji baaɗi nii e ɓerɗe mooɗon?
Wiide bonnguujo «Luutti maa njaafaama» e wiide ɗum «Imma, ɓam dengeleewo maa njahaa», koɗum hen ɓuri newaade?
Kaa, faa mi anndina on Ɓii Neɗɗo ana jogii baawɗe e aduna oo yaafaade luutti… Nden, o wii bonnguujo oo:
—Miɗo haalane: imma, ɓam dengeleewo maa, kootaa suudu maa.
Ɗon e ɗon gorko oo immii, ɓami dengeleewo mum witti, hedde yimɓe fuu ana ƴeewa ɗum. Ɓe fuu ɓe kaaynaa, ɓe ndarii eɓe njetta Laamɗo, eɓe mbiya: —Min njiyaali hono ɗum abada.
Iisaa wirfitii to weendu too. Jamaa oo fuu tawoyi mo ton, omo waajoo ɗum'en.
Nde o yahata ndee, o yii Lewi ɓii Alfaa ana jooɗii e duwaaɲeere mum, o wii ɗum: —Jokku e am! Lewi immii, jokki e makko.
Nde Iisaa ɲaamannoo e ley suudu Lewi ndee, duwaaɲe'en heewɓe e luuttooɓe hono mum'en njooɗii, ana ɲaamda e makko, kanko e taalibaaɓe makko. Sabi yimɓe heewɓe ana njokki e Iisaa.
Dunkee'en Sariya jeyaaɓe e waalde Farisa'en njii Iisaa ana ɲaamda e ɓeen yimɓe, mbii taalibaaɓe makko ɓee: —Ko saabii so omo ɲaamda e duwaaɲe'en, kaɲum e luuttooɓe hono mum'en?
Nde o nani ɗum ndee, o wii ɓe: —Wanaa celluɗo hasindini e cawroowo, ɲawɗo hasindini e cawroowo. Wanaa noddude fooccitiiɓe waddi kam, noddude luuttooɓe woni ko waddi kam.
Taalibaaɓe Yaayaa e Farisa'en ana koora. E ley ɗum, yimɓe ngari, lamndii Iisaa: —Ko saabii so taalibaaɓe Yaayaa e taalibaaɓe Farisa'en ana koora, kaa ɓe maa ɓee koorataa?
O jaabii ɓe, o wii: —Nootiiɓe kuurtungu ana mbaawi salaade ɲaamde tawa jommbaajo gorko oo ana wondi e mum'en naa? Mbaawaa. So nii jommbaajo gorko oo ana wondi e maɓɓe, ɓe mbaawaa salaade ɲaamde.
Kaa ɲalaaɗe ngaran ɗe jommbaajo gorko oo ittetee e hakkunde maɓɓe. E ɗeen ɲalaaɗe, ɓe kooran.
Fay gooto ɗammbataa fetalaare heyre e kaddungal kiinngal. So ɗum waɗii, fetalaare heyre ndee daamtan kaddungal kiinngal ngal, ceekol ngol ɓeydoo.
Kasen duu fay gooto loowataa peguujam kesam e sumalleeji kiiɗɗi. So ɗum waɗii peguujam ɗam fusan ɗi, kanjam e sumalleeji ɗii fuu mursidee. Peguujam kesam e sumalleeji kesi loowetee!
Waɗiino e ɲalaande fowteteende wootere, Iisaa ana seeka gese, taalibaaɓe mum ana kelta butaali e laawol ngol.
E ley ɗum, Farisa'en ɓee mbii mo: —Ƴeew, koɗum waɗi so taalibaaɓe maa ɓee ana ngolla ko dagaaki gollude ɲalaande fowteteende?
O jaabii ɓe, o wii: —Tama on meeɗaali janngude ko Daawuuda waɗi nde yolbi haajaa ko ɲaametee, kaɲum e yimɓe mum?
O naati e ley hukkum ceniiɗo oo e jamaanu Jottinoowo Sadaka Mawɗo biyeteeɗo Abiyataar, o ɲaami buuru cakkaaɗo oo, o hokki hen yimɓe makko. Tawee nee, yottinooɓe sadaka tan nduŋanaa ɲaamde oon buuru.
Iisaa wii ɓe kasen: —Ɲalaande fowteteende ndee kammari neɗɗo waɗiraa, wanaa neɗɗo waɗiraa kammari ɲalaande fowteteende ndee.
Ndennoo fay ɲalaande fowteteende ndee, Ɓii Neɗɗo woni joomum.
Iisaa naatti ley suudu waajordu nduu, o tawi ton gorko mo junngo mum waati.
Yimɓe wonnooɓe ɗon ɓee ngattani Iisaa hakkille. Ana ƴeewa yalla o anniyiiɗo sellinde gorko oo e ɲalaande fowteteende ndee, faa keɓa wullanaade mo.
Iisaa wii mo junngo mum waati oo: —Imma, dara hakkunde maɓɓe!
Caggal ɗum, o lamndii ɓe: —E ley ɲalaande fowteteende ana dagoo gollude ko moƴƴi naa gollude ko boni? Danndude neɗɗo naa warde ɗum? Kaa ɓe njaabaaki.
Iisaa ƴeewri ɓe tikkere, tiinndam-hoore maɓɓe ɗam woyni yonki makko, o wii gorko oo: —Fooccu junngo maa! Oon foocci ngo tan, ngo selli faa ngo warti hono no wonngo ngoo nii.
Ɗon e ɗon, Farisa'en ɓee njalti, njooddii e howruuɓe Hirudus faa ndawrida no mbarda Iisaa.
Caggal ɗum, o iwi ɗon, o fa'i weendu too, kanko e taalibaaɓe makko. Jamaa keewɗo iwɗo Galili jokki e makko.
Yimɓe heewɓe, iwɓe Yahuudiya e Urusaliima e Idumiya e leydi funnaange Urdun e seraaji Tirus e Sidon, nani ko o waɗannoo koo, ngari to makko.
Iisaa wii taalibaaɓe mum ɓee ndaarana ɗum laana pati jamaa oo ɓilla ɗum.
Saabe omo sellinannoo heewɓe waɗi so ɲawɓe ɓee fuu keɲanii mo yalla ana mema mo.
Wakkati mo seyɗaani'en njii mo fuu, ndiccoto, ngulla: —Aan a Ɓii Laamɗo!
Omo yagginannoo ɓe pati ɓe kumpita fay gooto kabaaru makko.
Caggal ɗum, o ŋabboyi dow waamnde haayre, o noddi ɓe o muuyi noddude, ɓeen ngari e makko.
O suɓii hen sappo e ɗiɗon, yalla ana ngonda e makko, o nela ɗum'en waajoyaade,
kasen o hokka ɗum'en baawɗe ribbude seyɗaani'en.
Ɓee ɗoo ngoni sappo e ɗiɗon ɓe o suɓii ɓee: Simon mo o innditiri Piyeer oo
e Yaakuuba e miɲum biyeteeɗo Yuhanna, ɓiɓɓe Jebede ɓe o innditiri Bowanerges ɓee (maanaa mum woni «nannduɓe e gidaango»)
kaɲum e Andire e Filipa e Bartolome e Matta e Tomaa e Yaakuuba ɓii Alfaa e Tadde e Simon kiranoowo suudu baaba
e Yahuuda Isikariyota jammbotooɗo mo oo.
Caggal ɗum, o hooti cuuɗi. Jamaa hawriti dow hoore makko kasen faa kanko e taalibaaɓe makko ɓe ndonki heɓude no ɓe ɲaamira.
Nde sakiraaɓe makko nani ɗum ndee, ngarani mo, sabi wiyaama hakkille makko sottii.
Dunkee'en Sariya iwnooɓe Urusaliima ngari, mbii: —Beelsebul woni e makko. Kasen ɓe mbii: —Oon woni hooreejo seyɗaani'en mo o ribbirta seyɗaani'en ɓee.
E ley ɗum, Iisaa noddi ɓe ɓe ngara e mum, haalaniri ɓe banndol, wii: —Hono Ibiliisa waawirta ribbude Ibiliisa?
So laamu fecciima ana haɓa e hoore mum, oon laamu waawataa heddaade.
Kasen duu so galle fecciima ana haɓa e hoore mum, oon galle waawataa heddaade.
Ndennoo, so Ibiliisa yanii e hoore mum fecciima, waawataa heddaade. Ko laatoto dee, kabaaru mum timman.
Iisaa jokkini hen: —Fay gooto waawaa naatude e galle gorko jom semmbe yaada e jawdi mum tawa haɓɓaali joomum tafon. Kaa so haɓɓii joomum faa teeŋii, ana waawi naɓude ko woni e galle mum fuu.
Miɗo haalana on goonga: yimɓe ana mbaawi yaafeede luutti mum'en fuu e bonkaaji ɗi ɓe mbonkii Laamɗo fuu.
Kaa bonkiiɗo Ruuhu Ceniiɗo oo heɓataa yaafaamuya fey, sabi joomum heddoto e luuttal mum faa abada.
Iisaa haaldii kaa haala saabe ko ɓe mbii omo wondi e seyɗaani koo.
Inna Iisaa e miɲiraaɓe Iisaa worɓe ngari, ndarii caggal galle oo, neli o noddee.
Ɗo jamaa oo filii mo ɗoo, wii mo: —Inna maa e miɲiraaɓe maa ana sella too, ana kaaje maa.
O jaabii, o wii: —Homo woni innam e miɲiraaɓe am?
O ƴeewi jooɗiiɓe so ana pilii mo ɓee, o wii: —Innam e miɲiraaɓe am annii.
Sabi gaɗoowo sago Laamɗo, kaɲum woni miɲam gorko, kaɲum woni miɲam debbo, kaɲum woni innam.
Iisaa ana waajoo dow fonngo weendu nduu kasen. Jamaa keewɗo filii mo faa o naati laana, o jooɗii. Jamaa oo fuu ana dow fonngo ngoo.
O darii omo waajoroo ɓe geɗe keewɗe e banndol, omo wiya ɓe:
—Kettinee! Aawoowo yalti aawoyde.
E ley sankugol ngol, yoga e aawdi ndii saami e laawol: pooli ngari cuɓi ɗum.
Yoga mayri saami e korokaaƴe ɗo leydi heewaano, fuɗi ɗon e ɗon, sabi aawdi ndii suddaaki gasa.
Kaa nde naange wulnoo ndee, sumi, yoori saabe walaa ɗaɗi.
Yoga mayri saami ɗo kebbe puɗata. Ndi fuɗidi e majje, ɗe cuumi ndi, ndi rimaali.
Yoga mayri saami e leydi mbelndi, fuɗi, mawni, rimi: yoga sowii cowe capantati, yoga capanɗe jeegom, yoga teemedere.
Caggal ɗum, o wii: —Jom nowru fuu yo nanu!
Nden Iisaa teelti, sappo e ɗiɗon ɓee e filinooɓe mo ɓee lamndii mo maanaa banndol ngol.
O wii ɓe: —Onon, on ndokkaama faamde goonga tedduɗo haala Laamu Laamɗo oo. Kaa wonɓe sella ɓee, huunde fuu e banndol kaalaniran-mi ɓe.
Ɗum waɗi so: «ana ƴeewa faa gasa tawa njiyataa, ana nana faa laaɓa paca tawa paamataa, sako ɓe tuuba so ɓe njaafee.»
O wii ɓe: —On paamaali ngol banndol naa? Hono paamirton banndi goɗɗi ɗii fuu ndennoo?
Aawoowo oo konngol Laamɗo o aawata.
Yimɓe yogaaɓe ana nanndi e laawol ɗo aawdi ndii saami ɗoo. Ɓe nanan konngol ngol, oon wakkati fuu Ibiliisa warata so itta konngol aawaangol e maɓɓe ngol.
Yogaaɓe ana nanndi e korokaaƴe ɗe aawdi ndii yuppii e muuɗum ɗee. Ɓe nanan konngol ngol, ɓe njaɓɓoroo ngol seyo oon wakkati fuu,
kaa ngol walaa ɗaɗi e maɓɓe, wakkati gooto tan ngol wonata e maɓɓe. Wakkati mo ɓillaare naa torra hewti ɓe saabe konngol ngol fuu, ɓe njankiran.
Yogaaɓe ɓee ana nanndi e nokku kebbe ɗo aawdi ndii saami ɗoo. Ɓee ngoni nanɓe konngol ngol,
kaa sugullaaji aduna e koomti jawdi, kaɲum e giɗaaɗe yonki goɗɗe naatan e maɓɓe, cuuma konngol ngol, ngol laatoo dimarol.
Kaa ɗo aawdi ndii saami e leydi lobbiri ɗoo, ɓee ngoni nanooɓe konngol ngol so njaɓa ngol. Ɓe ndiman: yoga sowoo cowe capantati, yoga capanɗe jeegom, yoga teemedere.
Caggal ɗum, Iisaa wii ɓe: —Won fuu kuɓɓoowo lampa so hippa hen saawal, naa soorna ɗum ley leeso? Wanaa sinndan ɗum naa?
Walaa fuu ko ɲooɓi ko ɓanngintaake, walaa ko suuɗii ko yaltintaake sella.
Jom nowru fuu yo nanu!
O wii ɓe kasen: —Tiiɗee e no nanirton haalaaji am ɗii nii! Sabi no etirton nii, non etirante-ɗon on ɓeydante duu.
Sabi jogiiɗo fuu ɓeydante, kaa mo walaa oo, fay seeɗa mo jogii oo teetete.
O wii kasen: —Laamu Laamɗo ana wa'i no neɗɗo cankuɗo aawdi e ngesa mum nii.
Caggal mum, ɗaanoo jemma daroo ɲalooma, no laatii fuu aawdi ndii fuɗan, mawna, tawa joomum anndaa no ndi mawniri.
Leydi ndii e hoore mum fuɗinta ndi, ndi waɗa gulle, wutaandu jokka hen, caggal ɗum, gabbe njokka hen.
So ko aawaa koo ɓenndii, o ɓaman wawdu makko o hetta, sabi wakkati mum yottike.
O jokkini hen: —Koɗum nanndinten e Laamu Laamɗo oo? Banndol hongol mbanndirten mo?
Laamu Laamɗo ana nanndi e ngeeƴu buyaage. Kaɲum ɓuri geeƴi ɗii fuu famɗude.
Kaa so mo aawaama, mo mawnan faa mo laatoo lekki mawki sanne, ki waɗa caɓe mawɗe faa pooli mbaawa ɲiɓude cuuɗi e ɗowdi makki.
Iisaa haalaniri yimɓe ɓee konngol Laamɗo ngol e banndi keewɗi baaɗi non, ko waarata e faamu maɓɓe.
O waajortaako so wanaa e banndol. Kaa nde o teeldi e taalibaaɓe makko ɓee fuu, o firritanan ɗum'en banndi ɗii fuu.
Kiikiiɗe oon ɲalooma, Iisaa wii taalibaaɓe mum ɓee: —Lummben, keedoyen ootoo bannge.
Ɓe njoppi jamaa oo, ɓe tawti mo e laana ka o wonnoo e mum kaa, ɓe ndeerti. Laanaaji goɗɗi duu ana njokki e makko.
Henndu sattundu immii, bempeeje immii ana piya laana kaa, faa ka hosi heewde ndiyam.
Kanko, omo ɗaanii to laaci laana too, omo wawlii mbawlu. Ɓe pinndini mo, ɓe mbii mo: —Moobbo, tama ko min kalkotoo koo wemmbaali ma?
O immii, o jahii e henndu nduu, o wii weendu nduu: —Deƴƴina! Wii teen! Henndu nduu deƴƴinii, fuu wii teen.
Caggal ɗum, o wii ɓe: —Ko saabii so kul-ɗon? Faa hannde on ngalaa hoolaare naa?
Ɓe kuli kulol cattungol hedde eɓe mbiyondira: —Homo oo gorko woni faa henndu e ndiyam ana ɗowtanoo ɗum?
Caggal ɗum, ɓe njottii oo too bannge e weendu nduu, e leydi Gerasankooɓe.
Nde Iisaa yalti laana kaa ndee, laddaaɗo iwri ley janaale, hawri e makko.
Ley janaale ɗee o jooɗinoo, fay gooto waawaa haɓɓude mo, sabi fay calali kaɓɓataa mo.
